Sūtrasthāna
rāgādirogān satatānuṣaktān aśeṣakāyaprasṛtān aśeṣān 
autsukyamohāratidāñ jaghāna yo 'pūrvavaidyāya namo 'stu tasmai   
āyuḥkāmayamānena dharmārthasukhasādhanam 
āyurvedopadeśeṣu vidheyaḥ param ādaraḥ   
brahmā smṛtvāyuṣo vedaṃ prajāpatim ajigrahat 
so 'śvinau tau sahasrākṣaṃ so 'triputrādikān munīn   
te 'gniveśādikāṃs te tu pṛthak tantrāṇi tenire 
tebhyo 'tiviprakīrṇebhyaḥ prāyaḥ sārataroccayaḥ   
kriyate 'ṣṭāṅgahṛdayaṃ nātisaṃkṣepavistaram 
kāyabālagrahordhvāṅgaśalyadaṃṣṭrājarāvṛṣān   
bv nātisaṃkṣiptavistṛtam
aṣṭāv aṅgāni tasyāhuś cikitsā yeṣu saṃśritā 
vāyuḥ pittaṃ kaphaś ceti trayo doṣāḥ samāsataḥ   
vikṛtāvikṛtā dehaṃ ghnanti te vartayanti ca 
te vyāpino 'pi hṛnnābhyor adhomadhyordhvasaṃśrayāḥ   
bv ghnanti te vardhayanti ca
vayo'horātribhuktānāṃ te 'ntamadhyādigāḥ kramāt 
tair bhaved viṣamas tīkṣṇo mandaś cāgniḥ samaiḥ samaḥ   
koṣṭhaḥ krūro mṛdur madhyo madhyaḥ syāt taiḥ samair api 
śukrārtavasthair janmādau viṣeṇeva viṣakrimeḥ   
taiś ca tisraḥ prakṛtayo hīnamadhyottamāḥ pṛthak 
samadhātuḥ samastāsu śreṣṭhā nindyā dvidoṣajāḥ   
cv samadhātuḥ samais tāsu
tatra rūkṣo laghuḥ śītaḥ kharaḥ sūkṣmaś calo 'nilaḥ 
pittaṃ sasnehatīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ laghu visraṃ saraṃ dravam   
snigdhaḥ śīto gurur mandaḥ ślakṣṇo mṛtsnaḥ sthiraḥ kaphaḥ 
saṃsargaḥ saṃnipātaś ca taddvitrikṣayakopataḥ   
rasāsṛṅmāṃsamedo'sthimajjaśukrāṇi dhātavaḥ 
sapta dūṣyā malā mūtraśakṛtsvedādayo 'pi ca   
vṛddhiḥ samānaiḥ sarveṣāṃ viparītair viparyayaḥ 
rasāḥ svādvamlalavaṇatiktoṣaṇakaṣāyakāḥ   
ṣaḍ dravyam āśritās te ca yathāpūrvaṃ balāvahāḥ 
tatrādyā mārutaṃ ghnanti trayas tiktādayaḥ kapham   
kaṣāyatiktamadhurāḥ pittam anye tu kurvate 
śamanaṃ kopanaṃ svasthahitaṃ dravyam iti tridhā   
uṣṇaśītaguṇotkarṣāt tatra vīryaṃ dvidhā smṛtam 
tridhā vipāko dravyasya svādvamlakaṭukātmakaḥ   
gurumandahimasnigdhaślakṣṇasāndramṛdusthirāḥ 
guṇāḥ sasūkṣmaviśadā viṃśatiḥ saviparyayāḥ   
kālārthakarmaṇāṃ yogo hīnamithyātimātrakaḥ 
samyagyogaś ca vijñeyo rogārogyaikakāraṇam   
rogas tu doṣavaiṣamyaṃ doṣasāmyam arogatā 
nijāgantuvibhāgena tatra rogā dvidhā smṛtāḥ   
teṣāṃ kāyamanobhedād adhiṣṭhānam api dvidhā 
rajas tamaś ca manaso dvau ca doṣāv udāhṛtau   
dv 'tra dvau doṣāv udāhṛtau
darśanasparśanapraśnaiḥ parīkṣeta ca rogiṇam 
rogaṃ nidānaprāgrūpalakṣaṇopaśayāptibhiḥ   
bv saṃparīkṣeta rogiṇam bv parīkṣetātha rogiṇam
bhūmidehaprabhedena deśam āhur iha dvidhā 
jāṅgalaṃ vātabhūyiṣṭham anūpaṃ tu kapholbaṇam   
sādhāraṇaṃ samamalaṃ tridhā bhūdeśam ādiśet 
kṣaṇādir vyādhyavasthā ca kālo bheṣajayogakṛt   
śodhanaṃ śamanaṃ ceti samāsād auṣadhaṃ dvidhā 
śarīrajānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ krameṇa paramauṣadham   
vastir vireko vamanaṃ tathā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu 
dhīdhairyātmādivijñānaṃ manodoṣauṣadhaṃ param   
bhiṣag dravyāṇy upasthātā rogī pādacatuṣṭayam 
cikitsitasya nirdiṣṭaṃ pratyekaṃ tac caturguṇam   
dakṣas tīrthāttaśāstrārtho dṛṣṭakarmā śucir bhiṣak 
bahukalpaṃ bahuguṇaṃ saṃpannaṃ yogyam auṣadham   
anuraktaḥ śucir dakṣo buddhimān paricārakaḥ 
āḍhyo rogī bhiṣagvaśyo jñāpakaḥ sattvavān api   
sādhyo 'sādhya iti vyādhir dvidhā tau tu punar dvidhā 
susādhyaḥ kṛcchrasādhyaś ca yāpyo yaś cānupakramaḥ   
sarvauṣadhakṣame dehe yūnaḥ puṃso jitātmanaḥ 
amarmago 'lpahetvagrarūparūpo 'nupadravaḥ   
atulyadūṣyadeśartuprakṛtiḥ pādasaṃpadi 
graheṣv anuguṇeṣv ekadoṣamārgo navaḥ sukhaḥ   
śastrādisādhanaḥ kṛcchraḥ saṃkare ca tato gadaḥ 
śeṣatvād āyuṣo yāpyaḥ pathyābhyāsād viparyaye   
anupakrama eva syāt sthito 'tyantaviparyaye 
autsukyamohāratikṛd dṛṣṭariṣṭo 'kṣanāśanaḥ   
tyajed ārtaṃ bhiṣagbhūpair dviṣṭaṃ teṣāṃ dviṣaṃ dviṣam 
hīnopakaraṇaṃ vyagram avidheyaṃ gatāyuṣam   
caṇḍaṃ śokāturaṃ bhīruṃ kṛtaghnaṃ vaidyamāninam 
tantrasyāsya paraṃ cāto vakṣyate 'dhyāyasaṃgrahaḥ   
āyuṣkāmadinartvīhārogānutpādanadravāḥ 
annajñānānnasaṃrakṣāmātrādravyarasāśrayāḥ   
doṣādijñānatadbhedataccikitsādvyupakramāḥ 
śuddhyādisnehanasvedarekāsthāpananāvanam   
dhūmagaṇḍūṣadṛksekatṛptiyantrakaśastrakam 
sirāvidhiḥ śalyavidhiḥ śastrakṣārāgnikarmikau   
cv sirāvyadhaḥ śalyavidhiḥ
sūtrasthānam ime 'dhyāyās triṃśac chārīram ucyate 
garbhāvakrāntitadvyāpadaṅgamarmavibhāgikam   
vikṛtir dūtajaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ nidānaṃ sārvarogikam 
jvarāsṛkśvāsayakṣmādimadādyarśo'tisāriṇām   
mūtrāghātapramehāṇāṃ vidradhyādyudarasya ca 
pāṇḍukuṣṭhānilārtānāṃ vātāsrasya ca ṣoḍaśa   
cikitsitaṃ jvare rakte kāse śvāse ca yakṣmaṇi 
vamau madātyaye 'rśaḥsu viṣi dvau dvau ca mūtrite   
vidradhau gulmajaṭharapāṇḍuśophavisarpiṣu 
kuṣṭhaśvitrānilavyādhivātāsreṣu cikitsitam   
dvāviṃśatir ime 'dhyāyāḥ kalpasiddhir ataḥ param 
kalpo vamer virekasya tatsiddhir vastikalpanā   
siddhir vastyāpadāṃ ṣaṣṭho dravyakalpo 'ta uttaram 
bālopacāre tadvyādhau tadgrahe dvau ca bhūtage   
unmāde 'tha smṛtibhraṃśe dvau dvau vartmasu saṃdhiṣu 
dṛktamoliṅganāśeṣu trayo dvau dvau ca sarvage   
karṇanāsāmukhaśirovraṇe bhaṅge bhagandare 
granthyādau kṣudrarogeṣu guhyaroge pṛthag dvayam   
viṣe bhujaṅge kīṭeṣu mūṣakeṣu rasāyane 
catvāriṃśo 'napatyānām adhyāyo bījapoṣaṇaḥ   
dv adhyāyo bījapoṣaṇe
ity adhyāyaśataṃ viṃśaṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ sthānair udīritam  ū 
Sūtrasthāna
brāhme muhūrta uttiṣṭhet svastho rakṣārtham āyuṣaḥ 
śarīracintāṃ nirvartya kṛtaśaucavidhis tataḥ   
arkanyagrodhakhadirakarañjakakubhādijam 
prātar bhuktvā ca mṛdvagraṃ kaṣāyakaṭutiktakam   
kanīnyagrasamasthaulyaṃ praguṇaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam 
bhakṣayed dantapavanaṃ dantamāṃsāny abādhayan   
cv bhakṣayed dantadhavanaṃ
nādyād ajīrṇavamathuśvāsakāsajvarārditī 
tṛṣṇāsyapākahṛnnetraśiraḥkarṇāmayī ca tat   
sauvīram añjanaṃ nityaṃ hitam akṣṇos tato bhajet 
cakṣus tejomayaṃ tasya viśeṣāc chleṣmato bhayam   
dv viśeṣāc chleṣmaṇo bhayam
bhuktavāṃś ca śiraḥsnātaḥ śrāntaḥ chardananāvanaiḥ 
rātrau jāgaritaś cāpi nāñjyāj jvarita eva ca   
yojayet saptarātre 'smāt srāvaṇārthaṃ rasāñjanam 
tato nāvanagaṇḍūṣadhūmatāmbūlabhāg bhavet   
bv srāvaṇārthe rasāñjanam
tāmbūlaṃ kṣatapittāsrarūkṣotkupitacakṣuṣām 
viṣamūrchāmadārtānām apathyaṃ śoṣiṇām api   
abhyaṅgam ācaren nityaṃ sa jarāśramavātahā 
dṛṣṭiprasādapuṣṭyāyuḥsvapnasutvaktvadārḍhyakṛt   
śiraḥśravaṇapādeṣu taṃ viśeṣeṇa śīlayet 
varjyo 'bhyaṅgaḥ kaphagrastakṛtasaṃśuddhyajīrṇibhiḥ   
lāghavaṃ karmasāmarthyaṃ dīpto 'gnir medasaḥ kṣayaḥ 
vibhaktaghanagātratvaṃ vyāyāmād upajāyate   
vātapittāmayī bālo vṛddho 'jīrṇo ca taṃ tyajet 
ardhaśaktyā niṣevyas tu balibhiḥ snigdhabhojibhiḥ   
śītakāle vasante ca mandam eva tato 'nyadā 
taṃ kṛtvānusukhaṃ dehaṃ mardayec ca samantataḥ   
tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ pratamako raktapittaṃ śramaḥ klamaḥ 
ativyāyāmataḥ kāso jvaraś chardiś ca jāyate   
vyāyāmajāgarādhvastrīhāsyabhāṣyādisāhasam 
gajaṃ siṃha ivākarṣan bhajann ati vinaśyati   
dv bhajan yato 'ti naśyati
udvartanaṃ kaphaharaṃ medasaḥ pravilāyanam 
sthirīkaraṇam aṅgānāṃ tvakprasādakaraṃ param   
dīpanaṃ vṛṣyam āyuṣyaṃ snānam ūrjābalapradam 
kaṇḍūmalaśramasvedatandrātṛḍdāhapāpmajit   
bv snānam ojobalapradam
uṣṇāmbunādhaḥkāyasya pariṣeko balāvahaḥ 
tenaiva tūttamāṅgasya balahṛtkeśacakṣuṣām   
cv tenaiva cottamāṅgasya cv sa eva cottamāṅgasya cv sa eva
tūttamāṅgasya
snānam arditanetrāsyakarṇarogātisāriṣu 
ādhmānapīnasājīrṇabhuktavatsu ca garhitam   
jīrṇe hitaṃ mitaṃ cādyān na vegān īrayed balāt 
na vegito 'nyakāryaḥ syān nājitvā sādhyam āmayam   
sukhārthāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ matāḥ sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ 
sukhaṃ ca na vinā dharmāt tasmād dharmaparo bhavet   
bhaktyā kalyāṇamitrāṇi sevetetaradūragaḥ 
hiṃsāsteyān yathākāmaṃ paiśunyaṃ paruṣānṛte   
saṃbhinnālāpaṃ vyāpādam abhidhyāṃ dṛgviparyayam 
pāpaṃ karmeti daśadhā kāyavāṅmānasais tyajet   
avṛttivyādhiśokārtān anuvarteta śaktitaḥ 
ātmavat satataṃ paśyed api kīṭapipīlikam   
arcayed devagovipravṛddhavaidyanṛpātithīn 
vimukhān nārthinaḥ kuryān nāvamanyeta nākṣipet   
upakārapradhānaḥ syād apakārapare 'py arau 
saṃpadvipatsv ekamanā hetāv īrṣyet phale na tu   
kāle hitaṃ mitaṃ brūyād avisaṃvādi peśalam 
pūrvābhibhāṣī sumukhaḥ suśīlaḥ karuṇāmṛduḥ   
naikaḥ sukhī na sarvatra viśrabdho na ca śaṅkitaḥ 
na kañcid ātmanaḥ śatruṃ nātmānaṃ kasyacid ripum   
prakāśayen nāpamānaṃ na ca niḥsnehatāṃ prabhoḥ 
janasyāśayam ālakṣya yo yathā parituṣyati   
av prakāśayen nāvamānaṃ
taṃ tathaivānuvarteta parārādhanapaṇḍitaḥ 
na pīḍayed indriyāṇi na caitāny ati lālayet   
trivargaśūnyaṃ nārambhaṃ bhajet taṃ cāvirodhayan 
anuyāyāt pratipadaṃ sarvadharmeṣu madhyamām   
nīcaromanakhaśmaśrur nirmalāṅghrimalāyanaḥ 
snānaśīlaḥ susurabhiḥ suveṣo 'nulbaṇojjvalaḥ   
cv snānaśīlaḥ sasurabhiḥ
dhārayet satataṃ ratnasiddhamantramahauṣadhīḥ 
sātapatrapadatrāṇo vicared yugamātradṛk   
niśi cātyayike kārye daṇḍī maulī sahāyavān 
caityapūjyadhvajāśastacchāyābhasmatuṣāśucīn   
nākrāmec charkarāloṣṭabalisnānabhuvo na ca 
nadīṃ taren na bāhubhyāṃ nāgniskandham abhivrajet   
saṃdigdhanāvaṃ vṛkṣaṃ ca nārohed duṣṭayānavat 
nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ kuryāt kṣutihāsyavijṛmbhaṇam   
dv kṣutiṃ hāsyaṃ vijṛmbhaṇam dv kṣuthāsyaṃ ca vijṛmbhaṇam
nāsikāṃ na vikuṣṇīyān nākasmād vilikhed bhuvam 
nāṅgaiś ceṣṭeta viguṇaṃ nāsītotkaṭakaś ciram   
bv nākasmād vilikhen mahīm dv nāsītotkaṭakasthitaḥ
dehavākcetasāṃ ceṣṭāḥ prāk śramād vinivartayet 
nordhvajānuś ciraṃ tiṣṭhen naktaṃ seveta na drumam   
tathā catvaracaityāntaścatuṣpathasurālayān 
sūnāṭavīśūnyagṛhaśmaśānāni divāpi na   
asaṃmārjitam ādarśam anupaskṛtakāminīm 
rajasvalāṃ ca nekṣeta sadā prātar amaṅgalam   
sarvathekṣeta nādityaṃ na bhāraṃ śirasā vahet 
nekṣeta pratataṃ sūkṣmaṃ dīptāmedhyāpriyāṇi ca   
madyavikrayasaṃdhānadānādānāni nācaret 
purovātātaparajastuṣāraparuṣānilān   
anṛjuḥ kṣavathūdgārakāsasvapnānnamaithunam 
kūlacchāyāṃ nṛpadviṣṭaṃ vyāladaṃṣṭriviṣāṇinaḥ   
hīnānāryātinipuṇasevāṃ vigraham uttamaiḥ 
saṃdhyāsv abhyavahārastrīsvapnādhyayanacintanam   
śatrusattragaṇākīrṇagaṇikāpaṇikāśanam 
gātravaktranakhair vādyaṃ hastakeśāvadhūnanam   
toyāgnipūjyamadhyena yānaṃ dhūmaṃ śavāśrayam 
madyātisaktiṃ viśrambhasvātantrye strīṣu ca tyajet   
ācāryaḥ sarvaceṣṭāsu loka eva hi dhīmataḥ 
anukuryāt tam evāto laukike 'rthe parīkṣakaḥ   
ārdrasaṃtānatā tyāgaḥ kāyavākcetasāṃ damaḥ 
svārthabuddhiḥ parārtheṣu paryāptam iti sadvratam   
naktandināni me yānti kathambhūtasya saṃprati 
duḥkhabhāṅ na bhavaty evaṃ nityaṃ saṃnihitasmṛtiḥ   
evaṃ kṛtsnadinaṃ nītvā rātrau yāme gṛhe gate 
devān ṛṣīn gurūn smṛtvā tataḥ śayanam ācaret   
bv rātrer yāme gate sati
ity ācāraḥ samāsena yaṃ prāpnoti samācaran 
āyur ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ yaśo lokāṃś ca śāśvatān   
Sūtrasthāna
māsair dvisaṃkhyair māghādyaiḥ kramāt ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ 
śiśiro 'tha vasantaś ca grīṣmo varṣāśaraddhimāḥ   
śiśirādyās tribhis tais tu vidyād ayanam uttaram 
ādānaṃ ca tad ādatte nṛṇāṃ pratidinaṃ balam   
tasmin hy atyarthatīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣā mārgasvabhāvataḥ 
ādityapavanāḥ saumyān kṣapayanti guṇān bhuvaḥ   
tiktaḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭuko balino 'tra rasāḥ kramāt 
tasmād ādānam āgneyam ṛtavo dakṣiṇāyanam   
varṣādayo visargaś ca yad balaṃ visṛjaty ayam 
saumyatvād atra somo hi balavān hīyate raviḥ   
meghavṛṣṭyanilaiḥ śītaiḥ śāntatāpe mahītale 
snigdhāś cehāmlalavaṇamadhurā balino rasāḥ   
śīte 'gryaṃ vṛṣṭigharme 'lpaṃ balaṃ madhyaṃ tu śeṣayoḥ 
balinaḥ śītasaṃrodhād dhemante prabalo 'nalaḥ   
bhavaty alpendhano dhātūn sa paced vāyuneritaḥ 
ato hime 'smin seveta svādvamlalavaṇān rasān   
dairghyān niśānām etarhi prātar eva bubhukṣitaḥ 
avaśyakāryaṃ saṃbhāvya yathoktaṃ śīlayed anu   
vātaghnatailair abhyaṅgaṃ mūrdhni tailaṃ vimardanam 
niyuddhaṃ kuśalaiḥ sārdhaṃ pādāghātaṃ ca yuktitaḥ   
bv mūrdhatailaṃ vimardanam
kaṣāyāpahṛtasnehas tataḥ snāto yathāvidhi 
kuṅkumena sadarpeṇa pradigdho 'gurudhūpitaḥ   
rasān snigdhān palaṃ puṣṭaṃ gauḍam acchasurāṃ surām 
godhūmapiṣṭamāṣekṣukṣīrotthavikṛtīḥ śubhāḥ   
navam annaṃ vasāṃ tailaṃ śaucakārye sukhodakam 
prāvārājinakauśeyapraveṇīkaucavāstṛtam   
dv praveṇīkuthakāstṛtam
uṣṇasvabhāvair laghubhiḥ prāvṛtaḥ śayanaṃ bhajet 
yuktyārkakiraṇān svedaṃ pādatrāṇaṃ ca sarvadā   
pīvarorustanaśroṇyaḥ samadāḥ pramadāḥ priyāḥ 
haranti śītam uṣṇāṅgyo dhūpakuṅkumayauvanaiḥ   
aṅgāratāpasaṃtaptagarbhabhūveśmacāriṇaḥ 
śītapāruṣyajanito na doṣo jātu jāyate   
ayam eva vidhiḥ kāryaḥ śiśire 'pi viśeṣataḥ 
tadā hi śītam adhikaṃ raukṣyaṃ cādānakālajam   
kaphaś cito hi śiśire vasante 'rkāṃśutāpitaḥ 
hatvāgniṃ kurute rogān atas taṃ tvarayā tyajet   
tīkṣṇair vamananasyādyair laghurūkṣaiś ca bhojanaiḥ 
vyāyāmodvartanāghātair jitvā śleṣmāṇam ulbaṇam   
snāto 'nuliptaḥ karpūracandanāgurukuṅkumaiḥ 
purāṇayavagodhūmakṣaudrajāṅgalaśūlyabhuk   
sahakārarasonmiśrān āsvādya priyayārpitān 
priyāsyasaṅgasurabhīn priyānetrotpalāṅkitān   
saumanasyakṛto hṛdyān vayasyaiḥ sahitaḥ pibet 
nirgadān āsavāriṣṭasīdhumārdvīkamādhavān   
śṛṅgaverāmbu sārāmbu madhvambu jaladāmbu ca 
dakṣiṇānilaśīteṣu parito jalavāhiṣu   
bv madhvambu jaladāmbu vā
adṛṣṭanaṣṭasūryeṣu maṇikuṭṭimakāntiṣu 
parapuṣṭavighuṣṭeṣu kāmakarmāntabhūmiṣu   
av adṛṣṭānaṣṭasūryeṣu
vicitrapuṣpavṛkṣeṣu kānaneṣu sugandhiṣu 
goṣṭhīkathābhiś citrābhir madhyāhnaṃ gamayet sukhī   
guruśītadivāsvapnasnigdhāmlamadhurāṃs tyajet 
tīkṣṇāṃśur atitīkṣṇāṃśur grīṣme saṃkṣipatīva yat   
cv sneham arko 'titīkṣṇāṃśur

Sūtrasthāna
jīvanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ hṛdyaṃ hlādi buddhiprabodhanam 
tanv avyaktarasaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ śītaṃ laghv amṛtopamam

bv śālyannaṃ rājatasthitam cv aklinnam avivarṇaṃ syāt cv
aklinnam avivarṇaṃ vā

nātiśleṣmakaro dhautaḥ sṛṣṭamūtraśakṛd guḍaḥ   
prabhūtakṛmimajjāsṛṅmedomāṃsakapho 'paraḥ 
hṛdyaḥ purāṇaḥ pathyaś ca navaḥ śleṣmāgnisādakṛt   
vṛṣyāḥ kṣīṇakṣatahitā raktapittānilāpahāḥ 
matsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍasitāḥ krameṇa guṇavattamāḥ   
tadguṇā tiktamadhurā kaṣāyā yāsaśarkarā 
dāhatṛṭchardimūrchāsṛkpittaghnyaḥ sarvaśarkarāḥ   
śarkarekṣuvikārāṇāṃ phāṇitaṃ ca varāvare 
cakṣuṣyaṃ chedi tṛṭśleṣmaviṣahidhmāsrapittanut   
mehakuṣṭhakṛmicchardiśvāsakāsātisārajit 
vraṇaśodhanasaṃdhānaropaṇaṃ vātalaṃ madhu   
rūkṣaṃ kaṣāyamadhuraṃ tattulyā madhuśarkarā 
uṣṇam uṣṇārtam uṣṇe ca yuktaṃ coṣṇair nihanti tat   
yakṣmārśo'rditapittāsṛṅnāśanaṃ grāhi dīpanam   
pracchardane nirūhe ca madhūṣṇaṃ na nivāryate 
alabdhapākam āśv eva tayor yasmān nivartate   
cv alabdhapākam evāśu
tailaṃ svayonivat tatra mukhyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vyavāyi ca 
tvagdoṣakṛd acakṣuṣyaṃ sūkṣmoṣṇaṃ kaphakṛn na ca   
kṛśānāṃ bṛṃhaṇāyālaṃ sthūlānāṃ karśanāya ca 
baddhaviṭkaṃ kṛmighnaṃ ca saṃskārāt sarvarogajit   
dv saṃskārāt sarvadoṣajit
satiktoṣaṇam airaṇḍaṃ tailaṃ svādu saraṃ guru 
vardhmagulmānilakaphān udaraṃ viṣamajvaram   
rukśophau ca kaṭīguhyakoṣṭhapṛṣṭhāśrayau jayet 
tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ picchilaṃ visraṃ raktairaṇḍodbhavaṃ tv ati   
kaṭūṣṇaṃ sārṣapaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ kaphaśukrānilāpaham 
laghu pittāsrakṛt koṭhakuṣṭhārśovraṇajantujit   
ākṣaṃ svādu himaṃ keśyaṃ guru pittānilāpaham 
nātyuṣṇaṃ nimbajaṃ tiktaṃ kṛmikuṣṭhakaphapraṇut   
umākusumbhajaṃ coṣṇaṃ tvagdoṣakaphapittakṛt 
vasā majjā ca vātaghnau balapittakaphapradau   
kaṣāyatiktakaṭukaṃ kārañjaṃ vraṇaśodhanam   
māṃsānugasvarūpau ca vidyān medo 'pi tāv iva 
dīpanaṃ rocanaṃ madhyaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ tuṣṭipuṣṭidam   
sasvādutiktakaṭukam amlapākarasaṃ saram 
sakaṣāyaṃ svarārogyapratibhāvarṇakṛl laghu   
naṣṭanidrātinidrebhyo hitaṃ pittāsradūṣaṇam 
kṛśasthūlahitaṃ rūkṣaṃ sūkṣmaṃ srotoviśodhanam   
vātaśleṣmaharaṃ yuktyā pītaṃ viṣavad anyathā 
guru taddoṣajananaṃ navaṃ jīrṇam ato 'nyathā   
drākṣekṣavaḥ sakharjūrāḥ śālipiṣṭam yavasya ca 
pañca madyākārāḥ śreṣṭhā drākṣā teṣāṃ viśiṣyate   
bv śāleḥ piṣṭam yavasya ca
peyaṃ noṣṇopacāreṇa na viriktakṣudhāturaiḥ 
nātyarthatīkṣṇamṛdvalpasaṃbhāraṃ kaluṣaṃ na ca   
gulmodarārśograhaṇīśoṣahṛt snehanī guruḥ 
surānilaghnī medo'sṛkstanyamūtrakaphāvahā   
tadguṇā vāruṇī hṛdyā laghus tīkṣṇā nihanti ca 
śūlakāsavamiśvāsavibandhādhmānapīnasān   
nātitīvramadā laghvī pathyā vaibhītakī surā 
vraṇe pāṇḍvāmaye kuṣṭhe na cātyarthaṃ virudhyate   
viṣṭambhinī yavasurā gurvī rūkṣā tridoṣalā 
yathādravyaguṇo 'riṣṭaḥ sarvamadyaguṇādhikaḥ   
grahaṇīpāṇḍukuṣṭhārśaḥśophaśoṣodarajvarān 
hanti gulmakṛmiplīhnaḥ kaṣāyakaṭuvātalaḥ   
dv kaṣāyaḥ kaṭuvātalaḥ
mārdvīkaṃ lekhanaṃ hṛdyaṃ nātyuṣṇaṃ madhuraṃ saram 
alpapittānilaṃ pāṇḍumehārśaḥkṛmināśanam   
asmād alpāntaraguṇaṃ khārjūraṃ vātalaṃ guru 
śārkaraḥ surabhiḥ svāduhṛdyo nātimado laghuḥ   
cv śārkaraṃ surabhi svādu dv hṛdyaṃ nātimadaṃ laghu
sṛṣṭamūtraśakṛdvāto gauḍas tarpaṇadīpanaḥ 
vātapittakaraḥ sīdhuḥ snehaśleṣmavikārahā   
medaḥśophodarārśoghnas tatra pakvaraso varaḥ 
chedī madhvāsavas tīkṣṇo mehapīnasakāsajit   
raktapittakaphotkledi śuktaṃ vātānulomanam 
bhṛśoṣṇatīkṣṇarūkṣāmlaṃ hṛdyaṃ rucikaraṃ saram   
dv hṛdyaṃ rucikaraṃ param
dīpanaṃ śiśirasparśaṃ pāṇḍudṛkkṛmināśanam 
guḍekṣumadyamārdvīkaśuktaṃ laghu yathottaram   
bv pāṇḍuhṛt kṛmināśanam cv guḍekṣumadyamādhvīka
kandamūlaphalādyaṃ ca tadvad vidyāt tadāsutam 
śāṇḍākī cāsutaṃ cānyat kālāmlaṃ rocanaṃ laghu   
dhānyāmlaṃ bhedi tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ pittakṛt sparśaśītalam 
śramaklamaharaṃ rucyaṃ dīpanaṃ vastiśūlanut   
śastam āsthāpane hṛdyaṃ laghu vātakaphāpaham 
ebhir eva guṇair yukte sauvīrakatuṣodake   
gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇād vaktramaladaurgandhyaśoṣajit   
kṛmihṛdrogagulmārśaḥpāṇḍuroganibarhaṇe 
te kramād vituṣair vidyāt satuṣaiś ca yavaiḥ kṛte   
av kṛmihṛdrogagulmārśo bv grahaṇīpāṇḍunāśane
mūtraṃ go'jāvimahiṣīgajāśvoṣṭrakharodbhavam 
pittalaṃ rūkṣatīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ kaṭu   
kṛmiśophodarānāhaśūlapāṇḍukaphānilān 
gulmāruciviṣaśvitrakuṣṭhārśāṃsi jayel laghu   
bv śūlapāṇḍukaphāmayān
toyakṣīrekṣutailānāṃ vargair madyasya ca kramāt 
iti dravaikadeśo 'yaṃ yathāsthūlam udāhṛtaḥ   
Sūtrasthāna
rakto mahān sakalamas tūrṇakaḥ śakunāhṛtaḥ 
sārāmukho dīrghaśūko lodhraśūkaḥ sugandhikaḥ   
puṇḍraḥ pāṇḍuḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ pramodo gauraśārivau 
kāñcano mahiṣaḥ śūkaḥ dūṣakaḥ kusumāṇḍakaḥ   
av pāṇḍukaḥ puṇḍarīkaś ca av pauṇḍrakaḥ puṇḍarīkaś ca bv
pramodo gauraśālikaḥ
lāṅgalā lohavālākhyāḥ kardamāḥ śītabhīrukāḥ 
pataṅgās tapanīyāś ca ye cānye śālayaḥ śubhāḥ   
av jāṅgalā lohavālākhyāḥ av lāṅgalā lohavālāś ca av lāṅgalo
lohavālākhyaḥ
bv kardamaḥ śītabhīrukaḥ
svādupākarasāḥ snigdhā vṛṣyā baddhālpavarcasaḥ 
kaṣāyānurasāḥ pathyā laghavo mūtralā himāḥ   
śūkajeṣu varas tatra raktas tṛṣṇātridoṣahā 
mahāṃs tam anu kalamas taṃ cāpy anu tataḥ pare   
cv mahāṃs tasyānu kalamas
yavakā hāyanāḥ pāṃsubāṣpanaiṣadhakādayaḥ 
svādūṣṇā guravaḥ snigdhāḥ pāke 'mlāḥ śleṣmapittalāḥ   
bv vāpyanaiṣadhakādayaḥ
sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāś ca pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ ca ninditāḥ 
snigdho grāhī laghuḥ svādus tridoṣaghnaḥ sthiro himaḥ   
ṣaṣṭiko vrīhiṣu śreṣṭho gauraś cāsitagaurataḥ 
tataḥ kramān mahāvrīhikṛṣṇavrīhijatūmukhāḥ   
kukkuṭāṇḍakalāvākhyapārāvatakaśūkarāḥ 
varakoddālakojjvālacīnaśāradadardurāḥ   
av kukkuṭāṇḍakapālākṣa av kukkuṭāṇḍakapālākhya av
kukkuṭāṇḍakalāvākṣa
dv cīnaśāradadurdarāḥ
gandhanāḥ kuruvindāś ca guṇair alpāntarāḥ smṛtāḥ 
svādur amlavipāko 'nyo vrīhiḥ pittakaro guruḥ   
bahumūtrapurīṣoṣmā tridoṣas tv eva pāṭalaḥ 
kaṅgukodravanīvāraśyāmākādi himaṃ laghu   
tṛṇadhānyaṃ pavanakṛl lekhanaṃ kaphapittahṛt 
bhagnasaṃdhānakṛt tatra priyaṅgur bṛṃhaṇī guruḥ   
koradūṣaḥ paraṃ grāhī sparśo śīto viṣāpahaḥ 
rūkṣaḥ śīto guruḥ svāduḥ saro viḍvātakṛd yavaḥ   
bv sparśo śīto garāpahaḥ bv sparśaśīto viṣāpahaḥ
vṛṣyaḥ sthairyakaro mūtramedaḥpittakaphāñ jayet 
pīnasaśvāsakāsorustambhakaṇṭhatvagāmayān   
nyūno yavād anuyavo rūkṣoṣṇo vaṃśajo yavaḥ 
vṛṣyaḥ śīto guruḥ snigdho jīvano vātapittahā   
av nyūno yāvad anyayavo
saṃdhānakārī madhuro godhūmaḥ sthairyakṛt saraḥ 
pathyā nandīmukhī śītā kaṣāyamadhurā laghuḥ   
niḥsārā vātalā rūkṣā jūrṇādhmānakarā sarā   
mudgāḍhakīmasūrādi śimbīdhānyaṃ vibandhakṛt 
kaṣāyaṃ svādu saṃgrāhi kaṭupākaṃ himaṃ laghu   
medaḥśleṣmāsrapitteṣu hitaṃ lepopasekayoḥ 
varo 'tra mudgo 'lpacalaḥ kalāyas tv ativātalaḥ   
asṛkpittaharo rūkṣo vātalaś caṇakaḥ smṛtaḥ   
rājamāṣo 'nilakaro rūkṣo bahuśakṛd guruḥ 
uṣṇāḥ kulatthāḥ pāke 'mlāḥ śukrāśmaśvāsapīnasān   
kāsārśaḥkaphavātāṃś ca ghnanti pittāsradāḥ param 
niṣpāvo vātapittāsrastanyamūtrakaro guruḥ   
cv niṣpāvo vātapittāsṛk
saro vidāhī dṛkśukrakaphaśophaviṣāpahaḥ 
māṣaḥ snigdho balaśleṣmamalapittakaraḥ saraḥ   
gurūṣṇo 'nilahā svāduḥ śukravṛddhivirekakṛt 
phalāni māṣavad vidyāt kākāṇḍolātmaguptayoḥ   
uṣṇas tvacyo himaḥ sparśe keśyo balyas tilo guruḥ 
alpamūtraḥ kaṭuḥ pāke medhāgnikaphapittakṛt   
av uṣṇas tvacyo himasparśaḥ
snigdhomā svādutiktoṣṇā kaphapittakarī guruḥ 
dṛkśukrahṛt kaṭuḥ pāke tadvad bījaṃ kusumbhajam   
māṣo 'tra sarveṣv avaro yavakaḥ śūkajeṣu ca 
navaṃ dhānyam abhiṣyandi laghu saṃvatsaroṣitam   
bv yavakaḥ śūkajeṣv api dv laghu varṣoṣitaṃ ca yat
śīghrajanma tathā sūpyaṃ nistuṣaṃ yuktibharjitam 
maṇḍapeyāvilepīnām odanasya ca lāghavam   
yavagodhūmamāṣāś ca tilāś cābhinavā hitāḥ 
purāṇā virasāḥ sūkṣmā na tathārthakarā matāḥ   
yathāpūrvaṃ śivas tatra maṇḍo vātānulomanaḥ 
tṛḍglānidoṣaśeṣaghnaḥ pācano dhātusāmyakṛt   
srotomārdavakṛt svedī saṃdhukṣayati cānalam 
kṣuttṛṣṇāglānidaurbalyakukṣirogajvarāpahā   
malānulomanī pathyā peyā dīpanapācanī 
vilepī grāhiṇī hṛdyā tṛṣṇāghnī dīpanī hitā   
vraṇākṣirogasaṃśuddhadurbalasnehapāyinām 
sudhautaḥ prasrutaḥ svinno 'tyaktoṣmā caudano laghuḥ   
yaś cāgneyauṣadhakvāthasādhito bhṛṣṭataṇḍulaḥ 
viparīto guruḥ kṣīramāṃsādyair yaś ca sādhitaḥ   
av yaś cāgneyauṣadhakvāthe bv sādhito bhṛṣṭataṇḍulaiḥ
iti dravyakriyāyogamānādyaiḥ sarvam ādiśet 
bṛṃhaṇaḥ prīṇano vṛṣyaś cakṣuṣyo vraṇahā rasaḥ   
maudgas tu pathyaḥ saṃśuddhavraṇakaṇṭhākṣirogiṇām 
vātānulomī kaulattho gulmatūṇīpratūṇijit   
akṛtaṃ kṛtayūṣaṃ ca tanu saṃskāritaṃ rasam 
sūpam amlam anamlaṃ ca guru vidyād yathottaram   
tilapiṇyākavikṛtiḥ śuṣkaśākaṃ virūḍhakam 
śāṇḍākīvaṭakaṃ dṛṅghnaṃ doṣalaṃ glapanaṃ guru   
rasālā bṛṃhaṇī vṛṣyā snigdhā balyā rucipradā 
śramakṣuttṛṭklamaharaṃ pānakaṃ prīṇanaṃ guru   
viṣṭambhi mūtralaṃ hṛdyaṃ yathādravyaguṇaṃ ca tat 
lājās tṛṭchardyatīsāramehamedaḥkaphacchidaḥ   
kāsapittopaśamanā dīpanā laghavo himāḥ 
pṛthukā guravo balyāḥ kaphaviṣṭambhakāriṇaḥ   
dhānā viṣṭambhinī rūkṣā tarpaṇī lekhanī guruḥ 
saktavo laghavaḥ kṣuttṛṭśramanetrāmayavraṇān   
dv śramanetragalāmayān
ghnanti saṃtarpaṇāḥ pānāt sadya eva balapradāḥ 
nodakāntaritān na dvir na niśāyāṃ na kevalān   
na bhuktvā na dvijaiś chittvā saktūn adyān na vā bahūn 
piṇyāko glapano rūkṣo viṣṭambhī dṛṣṭidūṣaṇaḥ   
raukṣyād viṣṭambhate koṣṭhe viṣṭambhitvād vidahyate 
vidāhāt kurute glāniṃ piṇyāko niśi sevitaḥ   
vesavāro guruḥ snigdho balopacayavardhanaḥ 
mudgādijās tu guravo yathādravyaguṇānugāḥ   
kukūlakarparabhrāṣṭrakandvaṅgāravipācitān 
ekayonī laghūn vidyād apūpān uttarottaram   
av kukūlakharparabhrāṣṭra bv kaṭvaṅgāravipācitān dv
apūpāṃs tu yathottaram
hariṇaiṇakuraṅgarkṣagokarṇamṛgamātṛkāḥ 
śaśaśambaracāruṣkaśarabhādyā mṛgāḥ smṛtāḥ   
lāvavārtīkavartīraraktavartmakakukkubhāḥ 
kapiñjalopacakrākhyacakorakurubāhavaḥ   
bv raktavartmakakurkubhāḥ
vartako vartikā caiva tittiriḥ krakaraḥ śikhī 
tāmracūḍākhyabakaragonardagirivartikāḥ   
cv kukkuṭo bakaraḥ kaṅka cv tāmracūḍākhyavaraka
tathā śārapadendrābhavaraṭādyāś ca viṣkirāḥ 
jīvañjīvakadātyūhabhṛṅgāhvaśukasārikāḥ   
bv vāraṭādyāś ca viṣkirāḥ bv vāraṭāś ceti viṣkirāḥ bv varaṭāś
ceti viṣkirāḥ
laṭvākokilahārītakapotacaṭakādayaḥ 
pratudā bhekagodhāhiśvāvidādyā bileśayāḥ   
gokharāśvataroṣṭrāśvadvīpisiṃharkṣavānarāḥ 
mārjāramūṣakavyāghravṛkababhrutarakṣavaḥ   
lopākajambukaśyenacāṣavāntādavāyasāḥ 
śaśaghnībhāsakuraragṛdhrolūkakuliṅgakāḥ   
cv śaśāribhāsakurara
dhūmikā madhuhā ceti prasahā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ 
varāhamahiṣanyaṅkurururohitavāraṇāḥ   
sṛmaraś camaraḥ khaḍgo gavayaś ca mahāmṛgāḥ 
haṃsasārasakādambabakakāraṇḍavaplavāḥ   
balākotkrośacakrāhvamadgukrauñcādayo 'pcarāḥ 
matsyā rohitapāṭhīnakūrmakumbhīrakarkaṭāḥ   
śuktiśaṅkhodraśambūkaśapharīvarmicandrikāḥ 
culūkīnakramakaraśiśumāratimiṅgilāḥ   
av śuktiśaṅkhodruśambūka cv cullakīnakramakara
rājīcilicimādyāś ca māṃsam ity āhur aṣṭadhā 
yoniṣv ajāvī vyāmiśragocaratvād aniścite   
mṛgyaṃ vaiṣkirikaṃ kiṃ ca prātudaṃ ca bileśayam 
prāsahaṃ ca mahāmṛgyam apcaraṃ mātsyam aṣṭadhā   
ādyāntyā jāṅgalānūpā madhyau sādhāraṇau smṛtau 
tatra baddhamalāḥ śītā laghavo jāṅgalā hitāḥ   
pittottare vātamadhye saṃnipāte kaphānuge 
dīpanaḥ kaṭukaḥ pāke grāhī rūkṣo himaḥ śaśaḥ   
īṣaduṣṇagurusnigdhā bṛṃhaṇā vartakādayaḥ 
tittiris teṣv api varo medhāgnibalaśukrakṛt   
grāhī varṇyo 'nilodriktasaṃnipātaharaḥ param 
nātipathyaḥ śikhī pathyaḥ śrotrasvaravayodṛśām   
tadvac ca kukkuṭo vṛṣyo grāmyas tu śleṣmalo guruḥ 
medhānalakarā hṛdyāḥ krakarāḥ sopacakrakāḥ   
guruḥ salavaṇaḥ kāṇakapotaḥ sarvadoṣakṛt 
caṭakāḥ śleṣmalāḥ snigdhā vātaghnāḥ śukralāḥ param   
dv vātaghnāḥ śukralāḥ bhṛśam
gurūṣṇasnigdhamadhurā vargāś cāto yathottaram 
mūtraśukrakṛto balyā vātaghnāḥ kaphapittalāḥ   
śītā mahāmṛgās teṣu kravyādaprasahāḥ punaḥ 
lavaṇānurasāḥ pāke kaṭukā māṃsavardhanāḥ   
bv kravyādāḥ prasahāḥ punaḥ
jīrṇārśograhaṇīdoṣaśoṣārtānāṃ paraṃ hitāḥ 
nātiśītagurusnigdhaṃ māṃsam ājam adoṣalam   
cv nātiśītaṃ guru snigdhaṃ
śarīradhātusāmānyād anabhiṣyandi bṛṃhaṇam 
viparītam ato jñeyam āvikaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ tu tat   
śuṣkakāsaśramātyagniviṣamajvarapīnasān 
kārśyaṃ kevalavātāṃś ca gomāṃsaṃ saṃniyacchati   
uṣṇo garīyān mahiṣaḥ svapnadārḍhyabṛhattvakṛt 
tadvad varāhaḥ śramahā ruciśukrabalapradaḥ   
matsyāḥ paraṃ kaphakarāś cilicīmas tridoṣakṛt 
lāvarohitagodhaiṇāḥ sve sve varge varāḥ param   
matsyādipakṣiṇāṃ caiva gurūṇy aṇḍāni cādiśet 
tāni snigdhāni vṛṣyāṇi svādupākarasāni ca   
bv gurūṇy aṇḍāny ato diśet bv gurūṇy aṇḍāni cānyato
māṃsaṃ sadyohataṃ śuddhaṃ vayaḥsthaṃ ca bhajet tyajet 
mṛtaṃ kṛśaṃ bhṛśaṃ medyaṃ vyādhivāriviṣair hatam   
puṃstriyoḥ pūrvapaścārdhe guruṇī garbhiṇī guruḥ 
laghur yoṣic catuṣpātsu vihaṅgeṣu punaḥ pumān

Sūtrasthāna
rājā rājagṛhāsanne prāṇācāryaṃ niveśayet 
sarvadā sa bhavaty evaṃ sarvatra pratijāgṛviḥ   
annapānaṃ viṣād rakṣed viśeṣeṇa mahīpateḥ 
yogakṣemau tadāyattau dharmādyā yannibandhanāḥ   
dv dharmādyās tannibandhanāḥ
odano viṣavān sāndro yāty avisrāvyatām iva 
cireṇa pacyate pakvo bhavet paryuṣitopamaḥ   
mayūrakaṇṭhatulyoṣmā mohamūrchāprasekakṛt 
hīyate varṇagandhādyaiḥ klidyate candrikācitaḥ   
dv klidyate candrikānvitaḥ dv klidyate candrakācitaḥ
dv klidyate candrakānvitaḥ
vyañjanāny āśu śuṣyanti dhyāmakvāthāni tatra ca 
hīnātiriktā vikṛtā chāyā dṛśyeta naiva vā   
dv chāyā dṛśyeta vā na vā
phenordhvarājisīmantatantubudbudasaṃbhavaḥ

cv vicchinnavirasā rāga cv vicchinnā virasā rāgāḥ dv khāṇḍavāḥ
śākam āmiṣam
nīlā rājī rase tāmrā kṣīre dadhani dṛśyate 
śyāvāpītāsitā takre ghṛte pānīyasaṃnibhā   
bv kṣīre dadhni ca dṛśyate
mastuni syāt kapotābhā rājī kṛṣṇā tuṣodake 
kālī madyāmbhasoḥ kṣaudre harit taile 'ruṇopamā   
pākaḥ phalānām āmānāṃ pakvānāṃ parikothanam

mṛdūnāṃ kaṭhinānāṃ ca bhavet sparśaviparyayaḥ 
mālyasya sphuṭitāgratvaṃ mlānir gandhāntarodbhavaḥ   
cv mālyānāṃ sphuṭitāgratvaṃ dv glānir gandhāntarodbhavaḥ dv
mlānigandhāntarodbhavaḥ
dhyāmamaṇḍalatā vastre śadanaṃ tantupakṣmaṇām 
dhātumauktikakāṣṭhāśmaratnādiṣu malāktatā   
bv śātanaṃ tantupakṣmaṇām
snehasparśaprabhāhāniḥ saprabhatvaṃ tu mṛnmaye

dv ekāvartaḥ sphuṭaty api
śikhikaṇṭhābhadhūmārcir anarcir vogragandhavān 
mriyante makṣikāḥ prāśya kākaḥ kṣāmasvaro bhavet

av udvejayati mārjāraḥ cv hṛṣyen mayūras tad dṛṣṭvā

yathā tena vipadyerann api na kṣudrajantavaḥ

spṛṣṭe tu kaṇḍūdāhoṣājvarārtisphoṭasuptayaḥ 
nakharomacyutiḥ śophaḥ sekādyā viṣanāśanāḥ

sasomavalkatālīśapattrakuṣṭhāmṛtānataiḥ

av lālā jihvauṣṭhayor jāḍyaṃ bv mukhe cimicimāyanam

āmāśayagate svedamūrchādhmānamadabhramāḥ

bindubhiś cācayo 'ṅgānāṃ pakvāśayagate punaḥ   
anekavarṇaṃ vamati mūtrayaty atisāryate

tayor vāntaviriktasya haridre kaṭabhīṃ guḍam 
sindhuvāritaniṣpāvabāṣpikāśataparvikāḥ   
taṇḍulīyakamūlāni kukkuṭāṇḍam avalgujam 
nāvanāñjanapāneṣu yojayed viṣaśāntaye

sūkṣmaṃ tāmrarajaḥ kāle sakṣaudraṃ hṛdviśodhanam

jāyate vipulaṃ cāyur gare 'py eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
viruddham api cāhāraṃ vidyād viṣagaropamam   
dv vidyād garaviṣopamam

uṣitāṃ niśām
dv nādyāt tām uṣitāṃ niśām dv kāmātām uṣitāṃ niśām dv
kāmācīm uṣitāṃ niśām

av matsyanistalanasneha bv sādhitāḥ pippalīs tyajet dv sarpir
uṣṇaṃ tv aruṣkaraiḥ
bhāso virudhyate śūlyaḥ kampillas takrasādhitaḥ 
aikadhyaṃ pāyasasurākṛśarāḥ parivarjayet   
madhusarpirvasātailapānīyāni dviśaś triśaḥ 
ekatra vā samāṃśāni virudhyante parasparam

madhupuṣkarabījaṃ ca madhumaireyaśārkaram

upodakātisārāya tilakalkena sādhitā

airaṇḍenāgninā siddhās tattailena vimūrchitāḥ

cv hāridravahninā sadyo
bhasmapāṃsuparidhvastaṃ tad eva ca samākṣikam 
yat kiñcid doṣam utkleśya na haret tat samāsataḥ   
viruddhaṃ śuddhir atreṣṭā śamo vā tadvirodhibhiḥ 
dravyais tair eva vā pūrvaṃ śarīrasyābhisaṃskṛtiḥ   
vyāyāmasnigdhadīptāgnivayaḥsthabalaśālinām

av vyāyāmisnigdhadīptāgni

sātmyāsātmyavikārāya jāyate sahasānyathā   
cv sātmyāsātmyaṃ vikārāya
krameṇāpacitā doṣāḥ krameṇopacitā guṇāḥ 
santo yānty apunarbhāvam aprakampyā bhavanti ca   
cv nāpnuvanti punarbhāvam
atyantasaṃnidhānānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ dūṣaṇātmanām 
ahitair dūṣaṇaṃ bhūyo na vidvān kartum arhati   
āhāraśayanābrahmacaryair yuktyā prayojitaiḥ 
śarīraṃ dhāryate nityam āgāram iva dhāraṇaiḥ   
bv caryair yuktyā niṣevitaiḥ
āhāro varṇitas tatra tatra tatra ca vakṣyate 
nidrāyattaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ puṣṭiḥ kārśyaṃ balābalam   
bv tatra tatra ca lakṣyate
vṛṣatā klībatā jñānam ajñānaṃ jīvitaṃ na ca 
akāle 'tiprasaṅgāc ca na ca nidrā niṣevitā   
sukhāyuṣī parākuryāt kālarātrir ivāparā 
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ snigdhaṃ prasvapanaṃ divā   
arūkṣam anabhiṣyandi tv āsīnapracalāyitam 
grīṣme vāyucayādānaraukṣyarātryalpabhāvataḥ   
cv grīṣme vātacayādāna
divāsvapno hito 'nyasmin kaphapittakaro hi saḥ 
muktvā tu bhāṣyayānādhvamadyastrībhārakarmabhiḥ   
krodhaśokabhayaiḥ klāntān śvāsahidhmātisāriṇaḥ 
vṛddhabālābalakṣīṇakṣatatṛṭśūlapīḍitān   
dv kṣuttṛṭśūlanipīḍitān
ajīrṇyabhihatonmattān divāsvapnocitān api 
dhātusāmyaṃ tathā hy eṣāṃ śleṣmā cāṅgāni puṣyati   
av ajīrṇābhihatonmattān
bahumedaḥkaphāḥ svapyuḥ snehanityāś ca nāhani 
viṣārtaḥ kaṇṭharogī ca naiva jātu niśāsv api   
akālaśayanān mohajvarastaimityapīnasāḥ 
śirorukśophahṛllāsasrotorodhāgnimandatāḥ   
tatropavāsavamanasvedanāvanam auṣadham 
yojayed atinidrāyāṃ tīkṣṇaṃ pracchardanāñjanam   
nāvanaṃ laṅghanaṃ cintāṃ vyavāyaṃ śokabhīkrudhaḥ 
ebhir eva ca nidrāyā nāśaḥ śleṣmātisaṃkṣayāt   
nidrānāśād aṅgamardaśirogauravajṛmbhikāḥ 
jāḍyaglānibhramāpaktitandrā rogāś ca vātajāḥ   
cv jāḍyaṃ glānibhramāpakti
kapho 'lpo vāyunoddhūto dhamanīḥ saṃnirudhya tu 
kuryāt saṃjñāpahāṃ tandrāṃ dāruṇāṃ mohakāriṇīm   
unmīlitavinirbhugne parivartitatārake 
bhavatas tatra nayane srute lulitapakṣmaṇī   
ardhatrirātrāt sā sādhyā na sā sādhyā tataḥ param  ab 
yathākālam ato nidrāṃ rātrau seveta sātmyataḥ 
asātmyāj jāgarād ardhaṃ prātaḥ svapyād abhuktavān   
cv asātmyajāgarād ardhaṃ
śīlayen mandanidras tu kṣīramadyarasān dadhi 
abhyaṅgodvartanasnānamūrdhakarṇākṣitarpaṇam   
kāntābāhulatāśleṣo nirvṛtiḥ kṛtakṛtyatā 
mano'nukūlā viṣayāḥ kāmaṃ nidrāsukhapradāḥ   
brahmacaryarater grāmyasukhaniḥspṛhacetasaḥ 
nidrā saṃtoṣatṛptasya svaṃ kālaṃ nātivartate   
grāmyadharme tyajen nārīm anuttānāṃ rajasvalām 
apriyām apriyācārāṃ duṣṭasaṃkīrṇamehanām   
atisthūlakṛśām sūtāṃ garbhiṇīm anyayoṣitam 
varṇinīm anyayoniṃ ca gurudevanṛpālayam   
bv garbhiṇīm anyayoṣitām
caityaśmaśānāyatanacatvarāmbucatuṣpatham 
parvāṇy anaṅgaṃ divasaṃ śirohṛdayatāḍanam   
atyāśito 'dhṛtiḥ kṣudvān duḥsthitāṅgaḥ pipāsitaḥ 
bālo vṛddho 'nyavegārtas tyajed rogī ca maithunam   
seveta kāmataḥ kāmaṃ tṛpto vājīkṛtām hime 
tryahād vasantaśaradoḥ pakṣād varṣānidāghayoḥ   
bv tṛpto vājīkarair hime bv tṛpto vājīkṛtair hime cv dvyahād
vasantaśaradoḥ
dv pakṣād vṛṣṭinidāghayoḥ
bhramaklamorudaurbalyabaladhātvindriyakṣayāḥ

av bhramaklamorudaurbalyaṃ bv baladhātvindriyakṣayaḥ
smṛtimedhāyurārogyapuṣṭīndriyayaśobalaiḥ 
adhikā mandajaraso bhavanti strīṣu saṃyatāḥ   
dv bhavanti strīṣu saṃyutāḥ
snānānulepanahimānilakhaṇḍakhādyaśītāmbudugdharasayūṣasurāprasannāḥ 
seveta cānu śayanaṃ viratau ratasya tasyaivam āśu vapuṣaḥ punar eti dhāma

Sūtrasthāna
mātrāśī sarvakālaṃ syān mātrā hy agneḥ pravartikā 
mātrāṃ dravyāṇy apekṣante gurūṇy api laghūny api   
gurūṇām ardhasauhityaṃ laghūnāṃ nātitṛptatā 
mātrāpramāṇaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ sukhaṃ yāvad vijīryati   
dv sukhaṃ yāvad dhi jīryate
bhojanaṃ hīnamātraṃ tu na balopacayaujase 
sarveṣāṃ vātarogāṇāṃ hetutāṃ ca prapadyate   
atimātraṃ punaḥ sarvān āśu doṣān prakopayet 
pīḍyamānā hi vātādyā yugapat tena kopitāḥ   
cv saṃpīḍyamānā vātādyā
āmenānnena duṣṭena tad evāviśya kurvate 
viṣṭambhayanto 'lasakaṃ cyāvayanto viṣūcikām   
adharottaramārgābhyāṃ sahasaivājitātmanaḥ 
prayāti nordhvaṃ nādhastād āhāro na ca pacyate   
āmāśaye 'lasībhūtas tena so 'lasakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
vividhair vedanodbhedair vāyvādibhṛśakopataḥ   
sūcībhir iva gātrāṇi vidhyatīti viṣūcikā 
tatra śūlabhramānāhakampastambhādayo 'nilāt   
pittāj jvarātisārāntardāhatṛṭpralayādayaḥ 
kaphāc chardyaṅgagurutāvāksaṅgaṣṭhīvanādayaḥ   
viśeṣād durbalasyālpavahner vegavidhāriṇaḥ 
pīḍitaṃ mārutenānnaṃ śleṣmaṇā ruddham antarā   
alasaṃ kṣobhitaṃ doṣaiḥ śalyatvenaiva saṃsthitam 
śūlādīn kurute tīvrāṃś chardyatīsāravarjitān   
bv śalyatveneva saṃsthitam
so 'laso 'tyarthaduṣṭās tu doṣā duṣṭāmabaddhakhāḥ 
yāntas tiryak tanuṃ sarvāṃ daṇḍavat stambhayanti cet   
daṇḍakālasakaṃ nāma taṃ tyajed āśukāriṇam 
viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇaśīlino viṣalakṣaṇam   
āmadoṣaṃ mahāghoraṃ varjayed viṣasaṃjñakam 
viṣarūpāśukāritvād viruddhopakramatvataḥ   
athāmam alasībhūtaṃ sādhyaṃ tvaritam ullikhet 
pītvā sogrāpaṭuphalaṃ vāry uṣṇaṃ yojayet tataḥ   
svedanaṃ phalavartiṃ ca malavātānulomanīm 
nāmyamānāni cāṅgāni bhṛśaṃ svinnāni veṣṭayet   
bv maladoṣānulomanīm
madanaṃ pippalī kuṣṭhaṃ vacā gaurāś ca sarṣapāḥ 
guḍakṣārasamāyuktā phalavartiḥ praśasyate   
viṣūcyām ativṛddhāyāṃ pārṣṇyor dāhaḥ praśasyate 
tadahaś copavāsyainaṃ viriktavad upācaret   
tīvrārtir api nājīrṇī pibec chūlaghnam auṣadham 
āmasanno 'nalo nālaṃ paktuṃ doṣauṣadhāśanam   
nihanyād api caiteṣāṃ vibhramaḥ sahasāturam 
jīrṇāśane tu bhaiṣajyaṃ yuñjyāt stabdhagurūdare   
bv vyāpattiḥ sahasāturam
doṣaśeṣasya pākārtham agneḥ saṃdhukṣaṇāya ca 
śāntir āmavikārāṇāṃ bhavati tv apatarpaṇāt   
trividhaṃ trividhe doṣe tat samīkṣya prayojayet 
tatrālpe laṅghanaṃ pathyaṃ madhye laṅghanapācanam   
bv tat samīkṣya prakalpayet
prabhūte śodhanaṃ tad dhi mūlād unmūlayen malān 
evam anyān api vyādhīn svanidānaviparyayāt   
cikitsed anubandhe tu sati hetuviparyayam 
tyaktvā yathāyathaṃ vaidyo yuñjyād vyādhiviparyayam   
tadarthakāri vā pakve doṣe tv iddhe ca pāvake 
hitam abhyañjanasnehapānavastyādi yuktitaḥ   
bv doṣe vṛddhe ca pāvake bv doṣe tv ṛddhe tu pāvake
ajīrṇaṃ ca kaphād āmaṃ tatra śopho 'kṣigaṇḍayoḥ 
sadyobhukta ivodgāraḥ prasekotkleśagauravam   
viṣṭabdham anilāc chūlavibandhādhmānasādakṛt 
pittād vidagdhaṃ tṛṇmohabhramāmlodgāradāhavat   
dv bhramāmlodgāradāhakṛt
laṅghanaṃ kāryam āme tu viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ bhṛśam 
vidagdhe vamanaṃ yad vā yathāvasthaṃ hitaṃ bhavet   
dv yathāvasthaṃ hitaṃ bhajet
garīyaso bhavel līnād āmād eva vilambikā 
kaphavātānubaddhāmaliṅgā tatsamasādhanā   
cv kaphavātānuviddhāma
aśraddhā hṛdvyathā śuddhe 'py udgāre rasaśeṣataḥ 
śayīta kiñcid evātra sarvaś cānāśito divā   
dv sarvaś cānaśito divā
svapyād ajīrṇī saṃjātabubhukṣo 'dyān mitaṃ laghu 
vibandho 'tipravṛttir vā glānir mārutamūḍhatā   
dv glānir mārutaśūlatā
ajīrṇaliṅgaṃ sāmānyaṃ viṣṭambho gauravaṃ bhramaḥ 
na cātimātram evānnam āmadoṣāya kevalam   
dviṣṭaviṣṭambhidagdhāmagururūkṣahimāśuci 
vidāhi śuṣkam atyambuplutaṃ cānnaṃ na jīryati   
upataptena bhuktaṃ ca śokakrodhakṣudādibhiḥ 
miśraṃ pathyam apathyaṃ ca bhuktaṃ samaśanaṃ matam   
bv śokakrodhakṣudhādibhiḥ bv krodhaśokabhayādibhiḥ
vidyād adhyaśanaṃ bhūyo bhuktasyopari bhojanam 
akāle bahu cālpaṃ vā bhuktaṃ tu viṣamāśanam   
trīṇy apy etāni mṛtyuṃ vā ghorān vyādhīn sṛjanti vā 
kāle sātmyaṃ śuci hitaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ laghu tanmanāḥ   
ṣaḍrasaṃ madhuraprāyaṃ nātidrutavilambitam 
snātaḥ kṣudvān viviktastho dhautapādakarānanaḥ   
tarpayitvā pitṝn devān atithīn bālakān gurūn 
pratyavekṣya tiraśco 'pi pratipannaparigrahān   
samīkṣya samyag ātmānam anindann abruvan dravam 
iṣṭam iṣṭaiḥ sahāśnīyāc chucibhaktajanāhṛtam   
bhojanaṃ tṛṇakeśādijuṣṭam uṣṇīkṛtaṃ punaḥ 
śākāvarānnabhūyiṣṭham atyuṣṇalavaṇaṃ tyajet   
kilāṭadadhikūcīkākṣāraśuktāmamūlakam 
kṛśaśuṣkavarāhāvigomatsyamahiṣāmiṣam   
bv kṣāraśuktāmlamūlakam
māṣaniṣpāvaśālūkabisapiṣṭavirūḍhakam 
śuṣkaśākāni yavakān phāṇitaṃ ca na śīlayet   
bv tilapiṣṭavirūḍhakam
śīlayec chāligodhūmayavaṣaṣṭikajāṅgalam 
suniṣaṇṇakajīvantībālamūlakavāstukam   
pathyāmalakamṛdvīkāpaṭolīmudgaśarkarāḥ 
ghṛtadivyodakakṣīrakṣaudradāḍimasaindhavam   
triphalāṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ niśi netrabalāya ca 
svāsthyānuvṛttikṛd yac ca rogocchedakaraṃ ca yat   
bisekṣumocacocāmramodakotkārikādikam 
adyād dravyaṃ guru snigdhaṃ svādu mandaṃ sthiraṃ puraḥ   
viparītam ataś cānte madhye 'mlalavaṇotkaṭam 
annena kukṣer dvāv aṃśau pānenaikaṃ prapūrayet   
āśrayaṃ pavanādīnāṃ caturtham avaśeṣayet 
anupānaṃ himaṃ vāri yavagodhūmayor hitam   
dadhni madye viṣe kṣaudre koṣṇaṃ piṣṭamayeṣu tu 
śākamudgādivikṛtau mastutakrāmlakāñjikam   
bv koṣṇaṃ piṣṭamayeṣu ca
surā kṛśānāṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ sthūlānāṃ tu madhūdakam 
śoṣe māṃsaraso madyaṃ māṃse svalpe ca pāvake   
bv sthūlānāṃ ca madhūdakam dv māṃseṣv alpe ca pāvake
vyādhyauṣadhādhvabhāṣyastrīlaṅghanātapakarmabhiḥ 
kṣīṇe vṛddhe ca bāle ca payaḥ pathyaṃ yathāmṛtam   
av vyādhyauṣadhādhvabhārastrī
viparītaṃ yad annasya guṇaiḥ syād avirodhi ca 
anupānaṃ samāsena sarvadā tat praśasyate   
anupānaṃ karoty ūrjāṃ tṛptiṃ vyāptiṃ dṛḍhāṅgatām 
annasaṃghātaśaithilyaviklittijaraṇāni ca   
nordhvajatrugadaśvāsakāsoraḥkṣatapīnase 
gītabhāṣyaprasaṅge ca svarabhede ca tad dhitam   
praklinnadehamehākṣigalarogavraṇāturāḥ 
pānaṃ tyajeyuḥ sarvaś ca bhāṣyādhvaśayanaṃ tyajet   
pītvā bhuktvātapaṃ vahniṃ yānaṃ plavanavāhanam  ab 
prasṛṣṭe viṇmūtre hṛdi suvimale doṣe svapathage  c 
viśuddhe codgāre kṣudupagamane vāte 'nusarati  d 
tathāgnāv udrikte viśadakaraṇe dehe ca sulaghau  e 
prayuñjītāhāraṃ vidhiniyamitaṃ kālaḥ sa hi mataḥ  f 
fv prayuñjītāhāraṃ vidhiniyamitaḥ kālaḥ sa hi mataḥ
Sūtrasthāna
dravyam eva rasādīnāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ te hi tadāśrayāḥ 
pañcabhūtātmakaṃ tat tu kṣmām adhiṣṭhāya jāyate   
ambuyonyagnipavananabhasām samavāyataḥ 
tannirvṛttir viśeṣaś ca vyapadeśas tu bhūyasā   
dv vyapadeśaś ca bhūyasā
tasmān naikarasaṃ dravyaṃ bhūtasaṃghātasaṃbhavāt 
naikadoṣās tato rogās tatra vyakto rasaḥ smṛtaḥ   
av tan naikabhūtajaṃ dravyaṃ
avyakto 'nurasaḥ kiñcid ante vyakto 'pi ceṣyate 
gurvādayo guṇā dravye pṛthivyādau rasāśraye   
raseṣu vyapadiśyante sāhacaryopacārataḥ 
tatra dravyaṃ gurusthūlasthiragandhaguṇolbaṇam   
pārthivaṃ gauravasthairyasaṃghātopacayāvaham 
dravaśītagurusnigdhamandasāndrarasolbaṇam   
dv mandasāndraguṇolbaṇam
āpyaṃ snehanaviṣyandakledaprahlādabandhakṛt 
rūkṣatīkṣṇoṣṇaviśadasūkṣmarūpaguṇolbaṇam   
āgneyaṃ dāhabhāvarṇaprakāśapavanātmakam 
vāyavyaṃ rūkṣaviśadalaghusparśaguṇolbaṇam   
raukṣyalāghavavaiśadyavicāraglānikārakam 
nābhasaṃ sūkṣmaviśadalaghuśabdaguṇolbaṇam   
bv vicāraglapanātmakam
sauṣiryalāghavakaraṃ jagaty evam anauṣadham 
na kiñcid vidyate dravyaṃ vaśān nānārthayogayoḥ   
dravyam ūrdhvagamaṃ tatra prāyo 'gnipavanotkaṭam 
adhogāmi ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhūmitoyaguṇādhikam   
iti dravyaṃ rasān bhedair uttaratropadekṣyate 
vīryaṃ punar vadanty eke guru snigdhaṃ himaṃ mṛdu   
av iti dravyaṃ raso bhedair
laghu rūkṣoṣṇatīkṣṇaṃ ca tad evaṃ matam aṣṭadhā 
carakas tv āha vīryaṃ tat kriyate yena yā kriyā   
cv carakas tv āha vīryaṃ tu dv yena yā kriyate kriyā
nāvīryaṃ kurute kiñcit sarvā vīryakṛtā hi sā 
gurvādiṣv eva vīryākhyā tenānvartheti varṇyate   
samagraguṇasāreṣu śaktyutkarṣavivartiṣu 
vyavahārāya mukhyatvād bahvagragrahaṇād api   
av samagraguṇasāratvāc bv chaktyutkarṣavivartanāt
ataś ca viparītatvāt saṃbhavaty api naiva sā 
vivakṣyate rasādyeṣu vīryaṃ gurvādayo hy ataḥ   
uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ dvidhaivānye vīryam ācakṣate 'pi ca 
nānātmakam api dravyam agnīṣomau mahābalau   
vyaktāvyaktaṃ jagad iva nātikrāmati jātu cit 
tatroṣṇaṃ bhramatṛḍglānisvedadāhāśupākitāḥ   
av vyaktāvyaktaṃ jagad idaṃ av vyaktāvyaktaṃ yathā viśvaṃ
śamaṃ ca vātakaphayoḥ karoti śiśiraṃ punaḥ 
hlādanaṃ jīvanaṃ stambhaṃ prasādaṃ raktapittayoḥ   
jāṭhareṇāgninā yogād yad udeti rasāntaram 
rasānāṃ pariṇāmānte sa vipāka iti smṛtaḥ   
svāduḥ paṭuś ca madhuram amlo 'mlaṃ pacyate rasaḥ 
tiktoṣaṇakaṣāyāṇāṃ vipākaḥ prāyaśaḥ kaṭuḥ   
rasair asau tulyaphalas tatra dravyaṃ śubhāśubham 
kiñcid rasena kurute karma pākena cāparam   
guṇāntareṇa vīryeṇa prabhāveṇaiva kiñcana 
yad yad dravye rasādīnāṃ balavattvena vartate   
abhibhūyetarāṃs tat tat kāraṇatvaṃ prapadyate 
viruddhaguṇasaṃyoge bhūyasālpaṃ hi jīyate   
rasaṃ vipākas tau vīryaṃ prabhāvas tāny apohati 
balasāmye rasādīnām iti naisargikaṃ balam   
bv prabhāvas tān vyapohati
rasādisāmye yat karma viśiṣṭaṃ tat prabhāvajam 
dantī rasādyais tulyāpi citrakasya virecanī   
madhukasya ca mṛdvīkā ghṛtaṃ kṣīrasya dīpanam 
iti sāmānyataḥ karma dravyādīnāṃ punaś ca tat   
vicitrapratyayārabdhadravyabhedena bhidyate 
svādur guruś ca godhūmo vātajid vātakṛd yavaḥ   
uṣṇā matsyāḥ payaḥ śītaṃ kaṭuḥ siṃho na śūkaraḥ  ū 
Sūtrasthāna
kṣmāmbho'gnikṣmāmbutejaḥkhavāyvagnyanilago'nilaiḥ 
dvayolbaṇaiḥ kramād bhūtair madhurādirasodbhavaḥ   
teṣāṃ vidyād rasaṃ svāduṃ yo vaktram anulimpati 
āsvādyamāno dehasya hlādano 'kṣaprasādanaḥ   
bv yo vaktram upalimpati
priyaḥ pipīlikādīnām amlaḥ kṣālayate mukham 
harṣaṇo romadantānām akṣibhruvanikocanaḥ   
bv amlaḥ srāvayate mukham
lavaṇaḥ syandayaty āsyaṃ kapolagaladāhakṛt 
tikto viśadayaty āsyaṃ rasanaṃ pratihanti ca   
dv rasanāṃ pratihanti ca
udvejayati jihvāgraṃ kurvaṃś cimicimāṃ kaṭuḥ 
srāvayaty akṣināsāsyaṃ kapolaṃ dahatīva ca   
kaṣāyo jaḍayej jihvāṃ kaṇṭhasrotovibandhakṛt 
rasānām iti rūpāṇi karmāṇi madhuro rasaḥ   
ājanmasātmyāt kurute dhātūnāṃ prabalaṃ balam 
bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇavarṇakeśendriyaujasām   
praśasto bṛṃhaṇaḥ kaṇṭhyaḥ stanyasaṃdhānakṛd guruḥ 
āyuṣyo jīvanaḥ snigdhaḥ pittānilaviṣāpahaḥ   
kurute 'tyupayogena sa medaḥśleṣmajān gadān 
sthaulyāgnisādasaṃnyāsamehagaṇḍārbudādikān   
bv sa medaḥkaphajān gadān
amlo 'gnidīptikṛt snigdho hṛdyaḥ pācanarocanaḥ 
uṣṇavīryo himasparśaḥ prīṇanaḥ kledano laghuḥ   
cv uṣṇavīryo himaḥ sparśe dv prīṇano bhedano laghuḥ
karoti kaphapittāsraṃ mūḍhavātānulomanaḥ 
so 'tyabhyastas tanoḥ kuryāc chaithilyaṃ timiraṃ bhramam   
bv mūḍhavātānulomanam
kaṇḍūpāṇḍutvavīsarpaśophavisphoṭatṛḍjvarān 
lavaṇaḥ stambhasaṃghātabandhavidhmāpano 'gnikṛt   
snehanaḥ svedanas tīkṣṇo rocanaś chedabhedakṛt 
so 'tiyukto 'srapavanaṃ khalatiṃ palitaṃ valīm   
tṛṭkuṣṭhaviṣavīsarpān janayet kṣapayed balam 
tiktaḥ svayam arociṣṇur aruciṃ kṛmitṛḍviṣam   
kuṣṭhamūrchājvarotkleśadāhapittakaphāñ jayet 
kledamedovasāmajjaśakṛnmūtropaśoṣaṇaḥ   
laghur medhyo himo rūkṣaḥ stanyakaṇṭhaviśodhanaḥ 
dhātukṣayānilavyādhīn atiyogāt karoti saḥ   
cv dhātukṣayaṃ calavyādhīn
kaṭur galāmayodardakuṣṭhālasakaśophajit 
vraṇāvasādanaḥ snehamedaḥkledopaśoṣaṇaḥ   
dīpanaḥ pācano rucyaḥ śodhano 'nnasya śoṣaṇaḥ 
chinatti bandhān srotāṃsi vivṛṇoti kaphāpahaḥ   
bv śodhano 'nnasya hāṣaṇaḥ
kurute so 'tiyogena tṛṣṇāṃ śukrabalakṣayam 
mūrchām ākuñcanaṃ kampaṃ kaṭīpṛṣṭhādiṣu vyathām   
av kurute so 'tivegena
kaṣāyaḥ pittakaphahā gurur asraviśodhanaḥ 
pīḍano ropaṇaḥ śītaḥ kledamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ   
āmasaṃstambhano grāhī rūkṣo 'ti tvakprasādanaḥ 
karoti śīlitaḥ so 'ti viṣṭambhādhmānahṛdrujaḥ   
tṛṭkārśyapauruṣabhraṃśasrotorodhamalagrahān 
ghṛtahemaguḍākṣoṭamocacocaparūṣakam   
bv srotorodhagalagrahān bv srotobandhamalagrahān
abhīruvīrāpanasarājādanabalātrayam 
mede catasraḥ parṇinyo jīvantī jīvakarṣabhau   
madhūkaṃ madhukaṃ bimbī vidārī śrāvaṇīyugam 
kṣīraśuklā tukākṣīrī kṣīriṇyau kāśmarī sahe   
cv kṣīraśuklā tavakṣīrī
kṣīrekṣugokṣurakṣaudradrākṣādir madhuro gaṇaḥ 
amlo dhātrīphalāmlīkāmātuluṅgāmlavetasam   
dāḍimaṃ rajataṃ takraṃ cukraṃ pālevataṃ dadhi 
āmram āmrātakaṃ bhavyaṃ kapitthaṃ karamardakam   
vṛkṣāmlakolalikucakośāmlātakadhanvanam 
mastudhānyāmlamadyāni jambīraṃ tilakaṇṭakam   
varaṃ sauvarcalaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ viḍaṃ sāmudram audbhidam 
romakaṃ pāṃsujaṃ sīsaṃ kṣāraś ca lavaṇo gaṇaḥ   
dv kṣārāś ca lavaṇo gaṇaḥ
tiktaḥ paṭolī trāyantī vālakośīracandanam 
bhūnimbanimbakaṭukātagarāguruvatsakam   
naktamāladvirajanīmustamūrvāṭarūṣakam 
pāṭhāpāmārgakāṃsyāyoguḍūcīdhanvayāsakam   
pañcamūlaṃ mahad vyāghryau viśālātiviṣā vacā 
kaṭuko hiṅgumaricakṛmijitpañcakolakam   
cv kaṭuko hiṅgumaricaṃ dv kṛmijitpañcakolakam
kuṭherādyā haritakāḥ pittaṃ mūtram aruṣkaram 
vargaḥ kaṣāyaḥ pathyākṣaṃ śirīṣaḥ khadiro madhu   
bv pittaṃ mūtram aruṣkaraḥ cv vargaḥ kaṣāyaḥ pathyākṣaḥ
kadambodumbaraṃ muktāpravālāñjanagairikam 
bālaṃ kapitthaṃ kharjūraṃ bisapadmotpalādi ca   
dv bisapadmotpalāni ca
madhuraṃ śleṣmalaṃ prāyo jīrṇāc chāliyavād ṛte 
mudgād godhūmataḥ kṣaudrāt sitāyā jāṅgalāmiṣāt   
prāyo 'mlaṃ pittajananaṃ dāḍimāmalakād ṛte 
apathyaṃ lavaṇaṃ prāyaś cakṣuṣo 'nyatra saindhavāt   
tiktaṃ kaṭu ca bhūyiṣṭham avṛṣyaṃ vātakopanam 
ṛte 'mṛtāpaṭolībhyāṃ śuṇṭhīkṛṣṇārasonataḥ   
kaṣāyaṃ prāyaśaḥ śītaṃ stambhanaṃ cābhayāṃ vinā 
rasāḥ kaṭvamlalavaṇā vīryeṇoṣṇā yathottaram   
bv stambhanaṃ cābhayāmṛte
tiktaḥ kaṣāyo madhuras tadvad eva ca śītalāḥ 
tiktaḥ kaṭuḥ kaṣāyaś ca rūkṣā baddhamalās tathā   
paṭvamlamadhurāḥ snigdhāḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtramārutāḥ 
paṭoḥ kaṣāyas tasmāc ca madhuraḥ paramaṃ guruḥ   
laghur amlaḥ kaṭus tasmāt tasmād api ca tiktakaḥ 
saṃyogāḥ saptapañcāśat kalpanā tu triṣaṣṭidhā   
lavaṇād amlamadhurau kāryau syātāṃ yathākramam 
vāyor niranubandhasya pākaśāntipravṛttaye   
dv pākaśāntiprasaktaye
prāk tikto madhuraḥ paścāt kaṣāyo 'nte vidhīyate 
taiḥ pittaṃ śamam abhyeti pakvācchīkṛtapiṇḍitam   
kaṭuḥ prāk tiktakaḥ paścāt kaṣāyo 'nte vidhīyate 
taiḥ śleṣmā śamam abhyeti pakvācchīkṛtapiṇḍitaḥ   
av kaṭukaḥ prāk tatas tiktaḥ dv pakvo 'cchīkṛtapiṇḍitaḥ
rasānāṃ yaugikatvena yathāsthūlaṃ vibhajyate 
ekaikahīnās tān pañcadaśa yānti rasā dvike   
cv ekaikahīnās te pañca dv pañca yānti rasā dvike
svādur dvikeṣu pañcāmlaś caturo lavaṇas trayam 
dvau tiktaḥ kaṭukaś caikaṃ yāti pañcadaśeti tu   
trike svādur daśāmlaḥ ṣaṭ trīn paṭus tikta ekakam 
catuṣkeṣu daśa svāduś caturo 'mlaḥ paṭuḥ sakṛt   
cv catuṣke tu daśa svāduś
pañcakeṣv ekam evāmlo madhuraḥ pañca sevate 
dravyam ekaṃ ṣaḍāsvādam asaṃyuktāś ca ṣaḍ rasāḥ   
ṣaṭ pañcakā ṣaṭ ca pṛthag rasāḥ syuś caturdvikau pañcadaśaprakārau 
bhedās trikā viṃśatir ekam eva dravyaṃ ṣaḍāsvādam iti triṣaṣṭiḥ   
te rasānurasato rasabhedās tāratamyaparikalpanayā ca 
saṃbhavanti gaṇanāṃ samatītā doṣabheṣajavaśād upayojyāḥ   
Sūtrasthāna
doṣadhātumalā mūlaṃ sadā dehasya taṃ calaḥ 
utsāhocchvāsaniśvāsaceṣṭāvegapravartanaiḥ   
samyaggatyā ca dhātūnām akṣāṇāṃ pāṭavena ca 
anugṛhṇāty avikṛtaḥ pittaṃ paktyūṣmadarśanaiḥ   
kṣuttṛḍruciprabhāmedhādhīśauryatanumārdavaiḥ 
śleṣmā sthiratvasnigdhatvasaṃdhibandhakṣamādibhiḥ   
prīṇanaṃ jīvanaṃ lepaḥ sneho dhāraṇapūraṇe 
garbhotpādaś ca dhātūnāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ karma kramāt smṛtam   
avaṣṭambhaḥ purīṣasya mūtrasya kledavāhanam 
svedasya kledavidhṛtir vṛddhas tu kurute 'nilaḥ   
cv svedasya keśavidhṛtir dv vṛddhaś ca kurute 'nilaḥ
kārśyakārṣṇyoṣṇakāmatvakampānāhaśakṛdgrahān 
balanidrendriyabhraṃśapralāpabhramadīnatāḥ   
av kārśyakārṣṇyoṣṇakāmitva
pītaviṇmūtranetratvakkṣuttṛḍdāhālpanidratāḥ 
pittaṃ śleṣmāgnisadanaprasekālasyagauravam   
śvaityaśaityaślathāṅgatvaṃ śvāsakāsātinidratāḥ 
raso 'pi śleṣmavad raktaṃ visarpaplīhavidradhīn   
kuṣṭhavātāsrapittāsragulmopakuśakāmalāḥ 
vyaṅgāgnināśasaṃmoharaktatvaṅnetramūtratāḥ   
cv vyaṅgāgnisādasaṃmoha
māṃsaṃ gaṇḍārbudagranthigaṇḍorūdaravṛddhitāḥ 
kaṇṭhādiṣv adhimāṃsaṃ ca tadvan medas tathā śramam   
bv gaṇḍorūdaravṛddhatāḥ
alpe 'pi ceṣṭite śvāsaṃ sphikstanodaralambanam 
asthy adhyasthy adhidantāṃś ca majjā netrāṅgagauravam   
cv mūtraṃ tu vaster nistodaṃ
parvasu sthūlamūlāni kuryāt kṛcchrāṇy arūṃṣi ca 
atistrīkāmatāṃ vṛddhaṃ śuktaṃ śukrāśmarīm api   
kukṣāv ādhmānam āṭopaṃ gauravaṃ vedanāṃ śakṛt 
mūtraṃ tu vastinistodaṃ kṛte 'py akṛtasaṃjñatām   
svedo 'tisvedadaurgandhyakaṇḍūr evaṃ ca lakṣayet 
dūṣikādīn api malān bāhulyagurutādibhiḥ   
liṅgaṃ kṣīṇe 'nile 'ṅgasya sādo 'lpaṃ bhāṣitehitam 
saṃjñāmohas tathā śleṣmavṛddhyuktāmayasaṃbhavaḥ   
pitte mando 'nalaḥ śītaṃ prabhāhāniḥ kaphe bhramaḥ 
śleṣmāśayānāṃ śūnyatvaṃ hṛddravaḥ ślathasaṃdhitā   
dv hṛdgadaḥ ślathasaṃdhitā
rase raukṣyaṃ śramaḥ śoṣo glāniḥ śabdāsahiṣṇutā 
rakte 'mlaśiśiraprītisirāśaithilyarūkṣatāḥ   
māṃse 'kṣaglānigaṇḍasphikśuṣkatāsaṃdhivedanāḥ 
medasi svapanaṃ kaṭyāḥ plīhno vṛddhiḥ kṛśāṅgatā   
asthny asthitodaḥ śadanaṃ dantakeśanakhādiṣu 
asthnāṃ majjani sauṣiryaṃ bhramas timiradarśanam   
av asthny asthitodaḥ sadanaṃ
śukre cirāt prasicyeta śukraṃ śoṇitam eva vā 
todo 'tyarthaṃ vṛṣaṇayor meḍhraṃ dhūmāyatīva ca   
purīṣe vāyur antrāṇi saśabdo veṣṭayann iva 
kukṣau bhramati yāty ūrdhvaṃ hṛtpārśve pīḍayan bhṛśam   
cv kukṣiṃ bhramati yāty ūrdhvaṃ
mūtre 'lpaṃ mūtrayet kṛcchrād vivarṇaṃ sāsram eva vā 
svede romacyutiḥ stabdharomatā sphuṭanaṃ tvacaḥ   
malānām atisūkṣmāṇāṃ durlakṣyaṃ lakṣayet kṣayam 
svamalāyanasaṃśoṣatodaśūnyatvalāghavaiḥ   
doṣādīnāṃ yathāsvaṃ ca vidyād vṛddhikṣayau bhiṣak 
kṣayeṇa viparītānāṃ guṇānāṃ vardhanena ca   
vṛddhiṃ malānāṃ saṅgāc ca kṣayaṃ cātivisargataḥ 
malocitatvād dehasya kṣayo vṛddhes tu pīḍanaḥ   
tatrāsthani sthito vāyuḥ pittaṃ tu svedaraktayoḥ 
śleṣmā śeṣeṣu tenaiṣām āśrayāśrayiṇāṃ mithaḥ   
yad ekasya tad anyasya vardhanakṣapaṇauṣadham 
asthimārutayor naivaṃ prāyo vṛddhir hi tarpaṇāt   
śleṣmaṇānugatā tasmāt saṃkṣayas tadviparyayāt 
vāyunānugato 'smāc ca vṛddhikṣayasamudbhavān   
vikārān sādhayec chīghraṃ kramāl laṅghanabṛṃhaṇaiḥ 
vāyor anyatra tajjāṃs tu tair evotkramayojitaiḥ   
viśeṣād raktavṛddhyutthān raktasrutivirecanaiḥ 
māṃsavṛddhibhavān rogān śastrakṣārāgnikarmabhiḥ   
sthaulyakārśyopacāreṇa medojān asthisaṃkṣayāt 
jātān kṣīraghṛtais tiktasaṃyutair vastibhis tathā   
dv saṃyuktair vastibhis tathā
majjaśukrodbhavān rogān bhojanaiḥ svādutiktakaiḥ 
vṛddhaṃ śukraṃ vyavāyādyair yac cānyac chukraśoṣikam   
av pratyanīkauṣadhaṃ majja bv śukravṛddhikṣaye hitam
viḍvṛddhijān atīsārakriyayā viṭkṣayodbhavān 
meṣājamadhyakulmāṣayavamāṣadvayādibhiḥ   
mūtravṛddhikṣayotthāṃś ca mehakṛcchracikitsayā 
vyāyāmābhyañjanasvedamadyaiḥ svedakṣayodbhavān   
av mūtravṛddhikṣayotthāṃs tu
svasthānasthasya kāyāgner aṃśā dhātuṣu saṃśritāḥ 
teṣāṃ sādātidīptibhyāṃ dhātuvṛddhikṣayodbhavaḥ   
pūrvo dhātuḥ paraṃ kuryād vṛddhaḥ kṣīṇaś ca tadvidham 
doṣā duṣṭā rasair dhātūn dūṣayanty ubhaye malān   
adho dve sapta śirasi khāni svedavahāni ca 
malā malāyanāni syur yathāsvaṃ teṣv ato gadāḥ   
ojas tu tejo dhātūnāṃ śukrāntānāṃ paraṃ smṛtam 
hṛdayastham api vyāpi dehasthitinibandhanam   
snigdhaṃ somātmakaṃ śuddham īṣallohitapītakam 
yannāśe niyataṃ nāśo yasmiṃs tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhati   
niṣpadyante yato bhāvā vividhā dehasaṃśrayāḥ 
ojaḥ kṣīyeta kopakṣuddhyānaśokaśramādibhiḥ   
bibheti durbalo 'bhīkṣṇaṃ dhyāyati vyathitendriyaḥ 
duśchāyo durmanā rūkṣo bhavet kṣāmaś ca tatkṣaye   
cv vicchāyo durmanā rūkṣo dv bhavet kṣāmaś ca tatkṣayāt
jīvanīyauṣadhakṣīrarasādyās tatra bheṣajam 
ojovṛddhau hi dehasya tuṣṭipuṣṭibalodayaḥ   
cv ojovṛddhau ca dehasya cv ojovṛddhau tu dehasya dv
tuṣṭipuṣṭibalodayāḥ
yad annaṃ dveṣṭi yad api prārthayetāvirodhi tu 
tat tat tyajan samaśnaṃś ca tau tau vṛddhikṣayau jayet   
cv tat tat tyajan samaśnan vā
kurvate hi ruciṃ doṣā viparītasamānayoḥ 
vṛddhāḥ kṣīṇāś ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ lakṣayanty abudhās tu na   
av kurvanti hi ruciṃ doṣā
yathābalaṃ yathāsvaṃ ca doṣā vṛddhā vitanvate 
rūpāṇi jahati kṣīṇāḥ samāḥ svaṃ karma kurvate   
ya eva dehasya samā vivṛddhyai ta eva doṣā viṣamā vadhāya 
yasmād atas te hitacaryayaiva kṣayād vivṛddher iva rakṣaṇīyāḥ   
dv kṣayād vivṛddher api rakṣaṇīyāḥ
Sūtrasthāna
pakvāśayakaṭīsakthiśrotrāsthisparśanendriyam 
sthānaṃ vātasya tatrāpi pakvādhānaṃ viśeṣataḥ   
nābhir āmāśayaḥ svedo lasīkā rudhiraṃ rasaḥ 
dṛk sparśanaṃ ca pittasya nābhir atra viśeṣataḥ   
uraḥkaṇṭhaśiraḥklomaparvāṇy āmāśayo rasaḥ 
medo ghrāṇaṃ ca jihvā ca kaphasya sutarām uraḥ   
prāṇādibhedāt pañcātmā vāyuḥ prāṇo 'tra mūrdhagaḥ 
uraḥkaṇṭhacaro buddhihṛdayendriyacittadhṛk   
ṣṭhīvanakṣavathūdgāraniḥśvāsānnapraveśakṛt 
uraḥ sthānam udānasya nāsānābhigalāṃś caret   
dv nāsānābhigalāṃś caran
vākpravṛttiprayatnorjābalavarṇasmṛtikriyaḥ 
vyāno hṛdi sthitaḥ kṛtsnadehacārī mahājavaḥ   
gatyapakṣepaṇotkṣepanimeṣonmeṣaṇādikāḥ 
prāyaḥ sarvāḥ kriyās tasmin pratibaddhāḥ śarīriṇām   
samāno 'gnisamīpasthaḥ koṣṭhe carati sarvataḥ 
annaṃ gṛhṇāti pacati vivecayati muñcati   
apāno 'pānagaḥ śroṇivastimeḍhrorugocaraḥ 
śukrārtavaśakṛnmūtragarbhaniṣkramaṇakriyaḥ   
pittaṃ pañcātmakaṃ tatra pakvāmāśayamadhyagam 
pañcabhūtātmakatve 'pi yat taijasaguṇodayāt   
tyaktadravyatvaṃ pākādikarmaṇānalaśabditam 
pacaty annaṃ vibhajate sārakiṭṭau pṛthak tathā   
dv sārakiṭṭe pṛthak tathā
tatrastham eva pittānāṃ śeṣāṇām apy anugraham 
karoti baladānena pācakaṃ nāma tat smṛtam   
āmāśayāśrayaṃ pittaṃ rañjakaṃ rasarañjanāt 
buddhimedhābhimānādyair abhipretārthasādhanāt   
sādhakaṃ hṛdgataṃ pittaṃ rūpālocanataḥ smṛtam 
dṛkstham ālocakaṃ tvaksthaṃ bhrājakaṃ bhrājanāt tvacaḥ   
śleṣmā tu pañcadhoraḥsthaḥ sa trikasya svavīryataḥ 
hṛdayasyānnavīryāc ca tatstha evāmbukarmaṇā   
av śleṣmāpi pañcadhoraḥsthaḥ
kaphadhāmnāṃ ca śeṣāṇāṃ yat karoty avalambanam 
ato 'valambakaḥ śleṣmā yas tv āmāśayasaṃsthitaḥ   
dv yas tv āmāśayasaṃśritaḥ
kledakaḥ so 'nnasaṃghātakledanād rasabodhanāt 
bodhako rasanāsthāyī śiraḥsaṃstho 'kṣatarpaṇāt   
tarpakaḥ saṃdhisaṃśleṣāc chleṣakaḥ saṃdhiṣu sthitaḥ 
iti prāyeṇa doṣāṇāṃ sthānāny avikṛtātmanām   
bv chleṣakaḥ saṃdhisaṃsthitaḥ
vyāpinām api jānīyāt karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak 
uṣṇena yuktā rūkṣādyā vāyoḥ kurvanti saṃcayam   
śītena kopam uṣṇena śamaṃ snigdhādayo guṇāḥ 
śītena yuktās tīkṣṇādyāś cayaṃ pittasya kurvate   
uṣṇena kopaṃ mandādyāḥ śamaṃ śītopasaṃhitāḥ 
śītena yuktāḥ snigdhādyāḥ kurvate śleṣmaṇaś cayam   
uṣṇena kopaṃ tenaiva guṇā rūkṣādayaḥ śamam 
cayo vṛddhiḥ svadhāmny eva pradveṣo vṛddhihetuṣu   
viparītaguṇecchā ca kopas tūnmārgagamitā 
liṅgānāṃ darśanaṃ sveṣām asvāsthyaṃ rogasaṃbhavaḥ   
svasthānasthasya samatā vikārāsaṃbhavaḥ śamaḥ 
cayaprakopapraśamā vāyor grīṣmādiṣu triṣu   
varṣādiṣu tu pittasya śleṣmaṇaḥ śiśirādiṣu 
cīyate laghurūkṣābhir oṣadhibhiḥ samīraṇaḥ   
av varṣādiṣu ca pittasya
tadvidhas tadvidhe dehe kālasyauṣṇyān na kupyati 
adbhir amlavipākābhir oṣadhibhiś ca tādṛśam   
pittaṃ yāti cayaṃ kopaṃ na tu kālasya śaityataḥ 
cīyate snigdhaśītābhir udakauṣadhibhiḥ kaphaḥ   
tulye 'pi kāle dehe ca skannatvān na prakupyati 
iti kālasvabhāvo 'yam āhārādivaśāt punaḥ   
bv skannatvān na vikupyati
cayādīn yānti sadyo 'pi doṣāḥ kāle 'pi vā na tu 
vyāpnoti sahasā deham āpādatalamastakam   
nivartate tu kupito malo 'lpālpaṃ jalaughavat 
nānārūpair asaṃkhyeyair vikāraiḥ kupitā malāḥ   
tāpayanti tanuṃ tasmāt taddhetvākṛtisādhanam 
śakyaṃ naikaikaśo vaktum ataḥ sāmānyam ucyate   
doṣā eva hi sarveṣāṃ rogāṇām ekakāraṇam 
yathā pakṣī paripatan sarvataḥ sarvam apy ahaḥ   
chāyām atyeti nātmīyāṃ yathā vā kṛtsnam apy adaḥ 
vikārajātaṃ vividhaṃ trīn guṇān nātivartate   
tathā svadhātuvaiṣamyanimittam api sarvadā 
vikārajātaṃ trīn doṣān teṣāṃ kope tu kāraṇam   
arthair asātmyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ kālaḥ karma ca duṣkṛtam 
hīnātimithyāyogena bhidyate tat punas tridhā   
hīno 'rthenendriyasyālpaḥ saṃyogaḥ svena naiva vā 
atiyogo 'tisaṃsargaḥ sūkṣmabhāsurabhairavam   
atyāsannātidūrasthaṃ vipriyaṃ vikṛtādi ca 
yad akṣṇā vīkṣyate rūpaṃ mithyāyogaḥ sa dāruṇaḥ   
dv mithyāyogaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
evam atyuccapūtyādīn indriyārthān yathāyatham 
vidyāt kālas tu śītoṣṇavarṣābhedāt tridhā mataḥ   
dv varṣabhedāt tridhā mataḥ
sa hīno hīnaśītādir atiyogo 'tilakṣaṇaḥ 
mithyāyogas tu nirdiṣṭo viparītasvalakṣaṇaḥ   
kāyavākcittabhedena karmāpi vibhajet tridhā 
kāyādikarmaṇo hīnā pravṛttir hīnasaṃjñakaḥ   
cv kāyādikarmaṇāṃ hīnā dv pravṛttir hīnasaṃjñikā
atiyogo 'tivṛttis tu vegodīraṇadhāraṇam 
viṣamāṅgakriyārambhapatanaskhalanādikam   
av atiyogo 'tivṛttiś ca
bhāṣaṇaṃ sāmibhuktasya rāgadveṣabhayādi ca 
karma prāṇātipātādi daśadhā yac ca ninditam   
mithyāyogaḥ samasto 'sāv iha vāmutra vā kṛtam 
nidānam etad doṣāṇāṃ kupitās tena naikadhā   
bv iha cāmutra vā kṛtam
kurvanti vividhān vyādhīn śākhākoṣṭhāsthisaṃdhiṣu 
śākhā raktādayas tvak ca bāhyarogāyanaṃ hi tat   
dv bāhyarogāyanaṃ hi sā
tadāśrayā maṣavyaṅgagaṇḍālajyarbudādayaḥ 
bahirbhāgāś ca durnāmagulmaśophādayo gadāḥ   
antaḥ koṣṭho mahāsrota āmapakvāśayāśrayaḥ 
tatsthānāḥ chardyatīsārakāsaśvāsodarajvarāḥ   
antarbhāgaṃ ca śophārśogulmavisarpavidradhi 
śirohṛdayavastyādimarmāṇy asthnāṃ ca saṃdhayaḥ   
dv marmāṇy asthnāṃ tu saṃdhayaḥ
tannibaddhāḥ sirāsnāyukaṇḍarādyāś ca madhyamaḥ 
rogamārgaḥ sthitās tatra yakṣmapakṣavadhārditāḥ   
mūrdhādirogāḥ saṃdhyasthitrikaśūlagrahādayaḥ 
sraṃsavyāsavyadhasvāp asādaruktodabhedanam   
saṅgāṅgabhaṅgasaṃkocavartaharṣaṇatarpaṇam 
kampapāruṣyasauṣiryaśoṣaspandanaveṣṭanam   
stambhaḥ kaṣāyarasatā varṇaḥ śyāvo 'ruṇo 'pi vā 
karmāṇi vāyoḥ pittasya dāharāgoṣmapākitāḥ   
svedaḥ kledaḥ srutiḥ kothaḥ sadanaṃ mūrchanaṃ madaḥ 
kaṭukāmlau rasau varṇaḥ pāṇḍurāruṇavarjitaḥ   
śleṣmaṇaḥ snehakāṭhinyakaṇḍūśītatvagauravam 
bandhopalepastaimityaśophāpaktyatinidratāḥ   
varṇaḥ śveto rasau svādulavaṇau cirakāritā 
ity aśeṣāmayavyāpi yad uktaṃ doṣalakṣaṇam   
darśanādyair avahitas tat samyag upalakṣayet 
vyādhyavasthāvibhāgajñaḥ paśyann ārtān pratikṣaṇam   
abhyāsāt prāpyate dṛṣṭiḥ karmasiddhiprakāśinī 
ratnādisadasajjñānaṃ na śāstrād eva jāyate   
av abhyāsāj jāyate dṛṣṭiḥ av abhyāsāt kevalaṃ dṛṣṭiḥ
dṛṣṭāpacārajaḥ kaścit kaścit pūrvāparādhajaḥ 
tatsaṃkarād bhavaty anyo vyādhir evaṃ tridhā smṛtaḥ   
bv kaścit pūrvāpacārajaḥ dv vyādhir evaṃ tridhā mataḥ
yathānidānaṃ doṣotthaḥ karmajo hetubhir vinā 
mahārambho 'lpake hetāv ātaṅko doṣakarmajaḥ   
vipakṣaśīlanāt pūrvaḥ karmajaḥ karmasaṃkṣayāt 
gacchaty ubhayajanmā tu doṣakarmakṣayāt kṣayam   
dvidhā svaparatantratvād vyādhayo 'ntyāḥ punar dvidhā 
pūrvajāḥ pūrvarūpākhyā jātāḥ paścād upadravāḥ   
yathāsvajanmopaśayāḥ svatantrāḥ spaṣṭalakṣaṇāḥ 
viparītās tato 'nye tu vidyād evaṃ malān api   
tā lakṣayed avahito vikurvāṇān pratijvaram 
teṣāṃ pradhānapraśame praśamo 'śāmyatas tathā   
paścāc cikitset tūrṇaṃ vā balavantam upadravam 
vyādhikliṣṭaśarīrasya pīḍākarataro hi saḥ   
av paścāc cikitset pūrvaṃ vā
vikāranāmākuśalo na jihrīyāt kadācana 
na hi sarvavikārāṇāṃ nāmato 'sti dhruvā sthitiḥ   
sa eva kupito doṣaḥ samutthānaviśeṣataḥ 
sthānāntarāṇi ca prāpya vikārān kurute bahūn   
tasmād vikāraprakṛtīr adhiṣṭhānāntarāṇi ca 
buddhvā hetuviśeṣāṃś ca śīghraṃ kuryād upakramam   
dūṣyaṃ deśaṃ balaṃ kālam analaṃ prakṛtiṃ vayaḥ 
sattvaṃ sātmyaṃ tathāhāram avasthāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ   
sūkṣmasūkṣmāḥ samīkṣyaiṣāṃ doṣauṣadhanirūpaṇe 
yo vartate cikitsāyāṃ na sa skhalati jātu cit   
gurvalpavyādhisaṃsthānaṃ sattvadehabalābalāt 
dṛśyate 'py anyathākāraṃ tasminn avahito bhavet   
guruṃ laghum iti vyādhiṃ kalpayaṃs tu bhiṣagbruvaḥ 
alpadoṣākalanayā pathye vipratipadyate   
bv kalayaṃs tu bhiṣagbruvaḥ bv kalpayaṃs tu bhiṣag dhruvam
tato 'lpam alpavīryaṃ vā guruvyādhau prayojitam 
udīrayettarāṃ rogān saṃśodhanam ayogataḥ   
śodhanaṃ tv atiyogena viparītaṃ viparyaye 
kṣiṇuyān na malān eva kevalaṃ vapur asyati   
dv kevalaṃ vapur apy ati
ato 'bhiyuktaḥ satataṃ sarvam ālocya sarvathā 
tathā yuñjīta bhaiṣajyam ārogyāya yathā dhruvam   
dv ārogyāya yathā bhavet
vakṣyante 'taḥ paraṃ doṣā vṛddhikṣayavibhedataḥ 
pṛthak trīn viddhi saṃsargas tridhā tatra tu tān nava   
cv pṛthak trīn viddhi saṃsargaṃ
trīn eva samayā vṛddhyā ṣaḍ ekasyātiśāyane 
trayodaśa samasteṣu ṣaḍ dvyekātiśayena tu   
dv ṣaḍ dvyekātiśayena ca
ekaṃ tulyādhikaiḥ ṣaṭ ca tāratamyavikalpanāt 
pañcaviṃśatim ity evaṃ vṛddhaiḥ kṣīṇaiś ca tāvataḥ   
cv pañcaviṃśatir ity evaṃ
ekaikavṛddhisamatākṣayaiḥ ṣaṭ te punaś ca ṣaṭ 
ekakṣayadvandvavṛddhyā saviparyayayāpi te   
bhedā dviṣaṣṭir nirdiṣṭās triṣaṣṭiḥ svāsthyakāraṇam  ab 
saṃsargād rasarudhirādibhis tathaiṣāṃ  c 
cv saṃsargād rasarudhirādibhis tathaitān
doṣāṃs tu kṣayasamatāvivṛddhibhedaiḥ  d 
dv doṣāṇāṃ kṣayasamatāvivṛddhibhedaiḥ
ānantyaṃ taratamayogataś ca yātān  e 
jānīyād avahitamānaso yathāsvam  f 
Sūtrasthāna
vātasyopakramaḥ snehaḥ svedaḥ saṃśodhanaṃ mṛdu 
svādvamlalavaṇoṣṇāni bhojyāny abhyaṅgamardanam   
veṣṭanaṃ trāsanaṃ seko madyaṃ paiṣṭikagauḍikam 
snigdhoṣṇā vastayo vastiniyamaḥ sukhaśīlatā   
dīpanaiḥ pācanaiḥ snigdhāḥ snehāś cānekayonayaḥ 
viśeṣān medyapiśitarasatailānuvāsanam   
pittasya sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ svāduśītair virecanam 
svādutiktakaṣāyāṇi bhojanāny auṣadhāni ca   
sugandhiśītahṛdyānāṃ gandhānām upasevanam 
kaṇṭheguṇānāṃ hārāṇāṃ maṇīnām urasā dhṛtiḥ   
karpūracandanośīrair anulepaḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe 
pradoṣaś candramāḥ saudhaṃ hāri gītaṃ himo 'nilaḥ   
ayantraṇasukhaṃ mitraṃ putraḥ saṃdigdhamugdhavāk 
chandānuvartino dārāḥ priyāḥ śīlavibhūṣitāḥ   
av ayantraṇamukhaṃ mitraṃ
śītāmbudhārāgarbhāṇi gṛhāṇy udyānadīrghikāḥ 
sutīrthavipulasvacchasalilāśayasaikate   
sāmbhojajalatīrānte kāyamāne drumākule 
saumyā bhāvāḥ payaḥ sarpir virekaś ca viśeṣataḥ   
bv kāyamānaṃ drumākule
śleṣmaṇo vidhinā yuktaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vamanarecanam 
annaṃ rūkṣālpatīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ kaṭutiktakaṣāyakam   
dīrghakālasthitaṃ madyaṃ ratiprītiḥ prajāgaraḥ 
anekarūpo vyāyāmaś cintā rūkṣaṃ vimardanam   
viśeṣād vamanaṃ yūṣaḥ kṣaudraṃ medoghnam auṣadham 
dhūmopavāsagaṇḍūṣā niḥsukhatvaṃ sukhāya ca   
upakramaḥ pṛthag doṣān yo 'yam uddiśya kīrtitaḥ 
saṃsargasaṃnipāteṣu taṃ yathāsvaṃ vikalpayet   
dv taṃ yathāsvaṃ prakalpayet
graiṣmaḥ prāyo marutpitte vāsantaḥ kaphamārute 
maruto yogavāhitvāt kaphapitte tu śāradaḥ   
caya eva jayed doṣaṃ kupitaṃ tv avirodhayan 
sarvakope balīyāṃsaṃ śeṣadoṣāvirodhataḥ   
prayogaḥ śamayed vyādhim ekaṃ yo 'nyam udīrayet 
nāsau viśuddhaḥ śuddhas tu śamayed yo na kopayet   
av prayogaḥ śamayed vyādhiṃ bv yo 'nyam anyam udīrayet
vyāyāmād ūṣmaṇas taikṣṇyād ahitācaraṇād api 
koṣṭhāc chākhāsthimarmāṇi drutatvān mārutasya ca   
doṣā yānti tathā tebhyaḥ srotomukhaviśodhanāt 
vṛddhyābhiṣyandanāt pākāt koṣṭhaṃ vāyoś ca nigrahāt   
tatrasthāś ca vilamberan bhūyo hetupratīkṣiṇaḥ 
te kālādibalaṃ labdhvā kupyanty anyāśrayeṣv api   
tatrānyasthānasaṃstheṣu tadīyām abaleṣu tu 
kuryāc cikitsāṃ svām eva balenānyābhibhāviṣu   
āgantuṃ śamayed doṣaṃ sthāninaṃ pratikṛtya vā 
prāyas tiryaggatā doṣāḥ kleśayanty āturāṃś ciram   
sādhāraṇaṃ vā kurvīta kriyām ubhayayoginīm   
kuryān na teṣu tvarayā dehāgnibalavit kriyām 
śamayet tān prayogeṇa sukhaṃ vā koṣṭham ānayet   
jñātvā koṣṭhaprapannāṃś ca yathāsannaṃ vinirharet 
srotorodhabalabhraṃśagauravānilamūḍhatāḥ   
dv gauravānilamūḍhatā
ālasyāpaktiniṣṭhīvamalasaṅgāruciklamāḥ 
liṅgaṃ malānāṃ sāmānāṃ nirāmāṇāṃ viparyayaḥ   
viṇmūtranakhadantatvakcakṣuṣāṃ pītatā bhavet 
raktatvam atha kṛṣṇatvaṃ pṛṣṭhāsthikaṭisaṃdhiruk   
dv pṛṣṭhāsthikaṭisaṃdhiṣu
śiroruk jāyate tīvrā nidrā virasatā mukhe 
kvacic ca śvayathur gātre jvarātīsāraharṣaṇam   
ūṣmaṇo 'lpabalatvena dhātum ādyam apācitam 
duṣṭam āmāśayagataṃ rasam āmaṃ pracakṣate   
anye doṣebhya evātiduṣṭebhyo 'nyo'nyamūrchanāt 
kodravebhyo viṣasyeva vadanty āmasya saṃbhavam   
āmena tena saṃpṛktā doṣā dūṣyāś ca dūṣitāḥ 
sāmā ity upadiśyante ye ca rogās tadudbhavāḥ   
vāyuḥ sāmo vibandhāgnisādastambhāntrakūjanaiḥ 
vedanāśophanistodaiḥ kramaśo 'ṅgāni pīḍayan   
vicared yugapac cāpi gṛhṇāti kupito bhṛśam 
snehādyair vṛddhim āyāti sūryameghodaye niśi   
nirāmo viśado rūkṣo nirvibandho 'lpavedanaḥ 
viparītaguṇaiḥ śāntiṃ snigdhair yāti viśeṣataḥ   
durgandhi haritaṃ śyāvaṃ pittam amlaṃ ghanaṃ guru 
amlīkākaṇṭhahṛddāhakaraṃ sāmaṃ vinirdiśet   
ātāmrapītam atyuṣṇaṃ rase kaṭukam asthiram 
pakvaṃ vigandhi vijñeyaṃ rucipaktibalapradam   
dv rucivahnibalapradam
āvilas tantulaḥ styānaḥ kaṇṭhadeśe 'vatiṣṭhate 
sāmo balāso durgandhiḥ kṣududgāravighātakṛt   
phenavān piṇḍitaḥ pāṇdur niḥsāro 'gandha eva ca 
pakvaḥ sa eva vijñeyaś chedavān vaktraśuddhidaḥ   
sarvadehapravisṛtān sāmān doṣān na nirharet 
līnān dhātuṣv anutkliṣṭān phalād āmād rasān iva   
āśrayasya hi nāśāya te syur durnirharatvataḥ 
pācanair dīpanaiḥ snehais tān svedaiś ca pariṣkṛtān   
śodhayec chodhanaiḥ kāle yathāsannaṃ yathābalam 
hanty āśu yuktaṃ vaktreṇa dravyam āmāśayān malān   
ghrāṇena cordhvajatrūtthān pakvādhānād gudena ca 
utkliṣṭān adha ūrdhvaṃ vā na cāmān vahataḥ svayam   
dhārayed auṣadhair doṣān vidhṛtās te hi rogadāḥ 
pravṛttān prāg ato doṣān upekṣeta hitāśinaḥ   
vibaddhān pācanais tais taiḥ pācayen nirhareta vā 
śrāvaṇe kārttike caitre māsi sādhāraṇe kramāt   
bv pācayen nirharet tathā
prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu māseṣv eteṣu śodhayet 
sādhāraṇeṣu vidhinā trimāsāntaritān malān   
grīṣmavarṣāhimacitān vāyvādīn āśu nirharet 
atyuṣṇavarṣaśītā hi grīṣmavarṣāhimāgamāḥ   
saṃdhau sādhāraṇe teṣāṃ duṣṭān doṣān viśodhayet 
svasthavṛttam abhipretya vyādhau vyādhivaśena tu   
trayaḥ sādhāraṇās teṣām antare prāvṛṣādayaḥ 
prāvṛṭ śucinabhau teṣu śarad ūrjasahau smṛtau   
tapasyo madhumāsaś ca vasantaḥ śodhanaṃ prati 
etān ṛtūn vikalpyaivaṃ dadyāt saṃśodhanaṃ bhiṣak   
kṛtvā śītoṣṇavṛṣṭīnāṃ pratīkāraṃ yathāyatham 
prayojayet kriyāṃ prāptāṃ kriyākālaṃ na hāpayet   
yuñjyād anannam annādau madhye 'nte kavaḍāntare 
grāse grāse muhuḥ sānnaṃ sāmudgaṃ niśi cauṣadham   
kaphodreke gade 'nannaṃ balino rogarogiṇoḥ 
annādau viguṇe 'pāne samāne madhya iṣyate   
vyāne 'nte prātarāśasya sāyamāśasya tūttare 
grāsagrāsāntayoḥ prāṇe praduṣṭe mātariśvani   
muhur muhur viṣacchardihidhmātṛṭśvāsakāsiṣu 
yojyaṃ sabhojyaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ bhojyaiś citrair arocake   
kampākṣepakahidhmāsu sāmudgaṃ laghubhojinām 
ūrdhvajatruvikāreṣu svapnakāle praśasyate   
Sūtrasthāna
upakramyasya hi dvitvād dvidhaivopakramo mataḥ 
ekaḥ saṃtarpaṇas tatra dvitīyaś cāpatarpaṇaḥ   
bṛṃhaṇo laṅghanaś ceti tatparyāyāv udāhṛtau 
bṛṃhaṇaṃ yad bṛhattvāya laṅghanaṃ lāghavāya yat   
dehasya bhavataḥ prāyo bhaumāpam itarac ca te 
snehanaṃ rūkṣaṇaṃ karma svedanaṃ stambhanaṃ ca yat   
bhūtānāṃ tad api dvaidhyād dvitayaṃ nātivartate 
śodhanaṃ śamanaṃ ceti dvidhā tatrāpi laṅghanam   
yad īrayed bahir doṣān pañcadhā śodhanaṃ ca tat 
nirūho vamanaṃ kāyaśiroreko 'sravisrutiḥ   
na śodhayati yad doṣān samān nodīrayaty api 
samīkaroti viṣamān śamanaṃ tac ca saptadhā   
pācanaṃ dīpanaṃ kṣuttṛḍvyāyāmātapamārutāḥ 
bṛṃhaṇaṃ śamanaṃ tv eva vāyoḥ pittānilasya ca   
bṛṃhayed vyādhibhaiṣajyamadyastrīśokakarśitān 
bhārādhvoraḥkṣatakṣīṇarūkṣadurbalavātalān   
garbhiṇīsūtikābālavṛddhān grīṣme 'parān api 
māṃsakṣīrasitāsarpirmadhurasnigdhavastibhiḥ   
svapnaśayyāsukhābhyaṅgasnānanirvṛtiharṣaṇaiḥ 
mehāmadoṣātisnigdhajvarorustambhakuṣṭhinaḥ   
visarpavidradhiplīhaśiraḥkaṇṭhākṣirogiṇaḥ 
sthūlāṃś ca laṅghayen nityaṃ śiśire tv aparān api   
tatra saṃśodhanaiḥ sthaulyabalapittakaphādhikān 
āmadoṣajvaracchardiratīsārahṛdāmayaiḥ   
vibandhagauravodgārahṛllāsādibhir āturān 
madhyasthaulyādikān prāyaḥ pūrvaṃ pācanadīpanaiḥ   
ebhir evāmayair ārtān hīnasthaulyabalādhikān 
kṣuttṛṣṇānigrahair doṣais tv ārtān madhyabalair dṛḍhān   
cv kṣuttṛṣṇānigrahair doṣair cv kṣuttṛṣṇānigrahair doṣaiś
dv cārtān madhyabalair dṛḍhān
samīraṇātapāyāsaiḥ kim utālpabalair narān 
na bṛṃhayel laṅghanīyān bṛṃhyāṃs tu mṛdu laṅghayet   
yuktyā vā deśakālādibalatas tān upācaret 
bṛṃhite syād balaṃ puṣṭis tatsādhyāmayasaṃkṣayaḥ   
vimalendriyatā sargo malānāṃ lāghavaṃ ruciḥ 
kṣuttṛṭsahodayaḥ śuddhahṛdayodgārakaṇṭhatā   
vyādhimārdavam utsāhas tandrānāśaś ca laṅghite 
anapekṣitamātrādisevite kurutas tu te   
atisthaulyātikārśyādīn vakṣyante te ca sauṣadhāḥ 
rūpaṃ tair eva ca jñeyam atibṛṃhitalaṅghite   
cv rūpaṃ tair eva vijñeyam
atisthaulyāpacīmehajvarodarabhagandarān 
kāsasaṃnyāsakṛcchrāmakuṣṭhādīn atidāruṇān   
tatra medo'nilaśleṣmanāśanaṃ sarvam iṣyate 
kulatthajūrṇaśyāmākayavamudgamadhūdakam   
mastudaṇḍāhatāriṣṭacintāśodhanajāgaram 
madhunā triphalāṃ lihyād guḍūcīm abhayāṃ ghanam   
rasāñjanasya mahataḥ pañcamūlasya gugguloḥ 
śilājatuprayogaś ca sāgnimantharaso hitaḥ   
cv śilāhvasya prayogaś ca
viḍaṅgaṃ nāgaraṃ kṣāraḥ kālaloharajo madhu 
yavāmalakacūrṇaṃ ca yogo 'tisthaulyadoṣajit   
vyoṣakaṭvīvarāśigruviḍaṅgātiviṣāsthirāḥ 
hiṅgusauvarcalājājīyavānīdhānyacitrakāḥ   
niśe bṛhatyau hapuṣā pāṭhā mūlaṃ ca kembukāt 
eṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca sadṛśāṃśakam   
dv tailaṃ ca sadṛśāṃśikam
saktubhiḥ ṣoḍaśaguṇair yuktaṃ pītaṃ nihanti tat 
atisthaulyādikān sarvān rogān anyāṃś ca tadvidhān   
hṛdrogakāmalāśvitraśvāsakāsagalagrahān 
buddhimedhāsmṛtikaraṃ saṃnasyāgneś ca dīpanam   
atikārśyaṃ bhramaḥ kāsas tṛṣṇādhikyam arocakaḥ 
snehāgninidrādṛkśrotraśukraujaḥkṣutsvarakṣayaḥ   
av atikārśyaṃ bhramaḥ śvāsa bv tṛṣṇādhikyam arocakaḥ
vastihṛnmūrdhajaṅghorutrikapārśvarujā jvaraḥ 
pralāpordhvānilaglānicchardiparvāsthibhedanam   
dv cchardiḥparvāsthibhedanam
varcomūtragrahādyāś ca jāyante 'tivilaṅghanāt 
kārśyam eva varaṃ sthaulyān na hi sthūlasya bheṣajam   
av viṇmūtrādigrahādyāś ca dv na hi sthaulyasya bheṣajam
bṛṃhaṇaṃ laṅghanaṃ vālam atimedo'gnivātajit 
madhurasnigdhasauhityair yat saukhyena ca naśyati   
av bṛṃhaṇaṃ laṅghanaṃ nālam cv madhurasnehasauhityair
dv yat saukhyena vinaśyati
kraśimā sthavimātyantaviparītaniṣevaṇaiḥ 
yojayed bṛṃhaṇaṃ tatra sarvaṃ pānānnabheṣajam   
acintayā harṣaṇena dhruvaṃ saṃtarpaṇena ca 
svapnaprasaṅgāc ca kṛśo varāha iva puṣyati   
av acintayā praharṣeṇa cv svapnaprasaṅgāc ca naro
na hi māṃsasamaṃ kiñcid anyad dehabṛhattvakṛt 
māṃsādamāṃsaṃ māṃsena saṃbhṛtatvād viśeṣataḥ   
dv saṃbhṛtatvād viśiṣyate dv saṃbhṛtatvād bṛhattvakṛt
guru cātarpaṇaṃ sthūle viparītaṃ hitaṃ kṛśe 
yavagodhūmam ubhayos tadyogyāhitakalpanam   
dv tadyogyahitakalpanam dv tato grāhitakalpanam
doṣagatyātiricyante grāhibhedyādibhedataḥ 
upakramā na te dvitvād bhinnā api gadā iva   
cv upakramā na tu dvitvād
Sūtrasthāna
madanamadhukalambānimbabimbīviśālātrapusakuṭajamūrvādevadālīkṛmighnam 
viduladahanacitrāḥ kośavatyau karañjaḥ kaṇalavaṇavacailāsarṣapāś chardanāni   
nikumbhakumbhatriphalāgavākṣīsnukśaṅkhinīnīlinitilvakāni 
śamyākakampillakahemadugdhā dugdhaṃ ca mūtraṃ ca virecanāni   
madanakuṭajakuṣṭhadevadālīmadhukavacādaśamūladārurāsnāḥ 
yavamiśikṛtavedhanaṃ kulatthā madhu lavaṇaṃ trivṛtā nirūhaṇāni   
cv yavamiśikṛtavedhanaṃ kulattho
vellāpāmārgavyoṣadārvīsurālā bījaṃ śairīṣaṃ bārhataṃ śaigravaṃ ca 
sāro mādhūkaḥ saindhavaṃ tārkṣyaśailaṃ truṭyau pṛthvīkā śodhayanty uttamāṅgam   
bhadradāru nataṃ kuṣṭhaṃ daśamūlaṃ balādvayam 
vāyuṃ vīratarādiś ca vidāryādiś ca nāśayet   
bv daśamūlaṃ balātrayam dv vidāryādiś ca śodhayet
dūrvānantā nimbavāsātmaguptā gundrābhīruḥ śītapākī priyaṅguḥ 
nyagrodhādiḥ padmakādiḥ sthire dve padmaṃ vanyaṃ śārivādiś ca pittam   
āragvadhādir arkādir muṣkakādyo 'sanādikaḥ 
surasādiḥ samustādir vatsakādir balāsajit   
jīvantīkākolyau mede dve mudgamāṣaparṇyau ca 
ṛṣabhakajīvakamadhukaṃ ceti gaṇo jīvanīyākhyaḥ   
vidāripañcāṅgulavṛścikālīvṛścīvadevāhvayaśūrpaparṇyaḥ 
kaṇḍūkarī jīvanahrasvasaṃjñe dve pañcake gopasutā tripādī   
bv vṛścīvadevādvayaśūrpaparṇyaḥ dv kaṇḍūkarī gopasutā tripādī
vidāryādir ayaṃ hṛdyo bṛṃhaṇo vātapittahā 
śoṣagulmāṅgamardordhvaśvāsakāsaharo gaṇaḥ   
cv śoṣagulmāṅgasādordhva
śārivośīrakāśmaryamadhūkaśiśiradvayam 
yaṣṭī parūṣakaṃ hanti dāhapittāsratṛḍjvarān   
padmakapuṇḍrau vṛddhitugarddhyaḥ śṛṅgy amṛtā daśa jīvanasaṃjñāḥ 
stanyakarā ghnantīraṇapittaṃ prīṇanajīvanabṛṃhaṇavṛṣyāḥ   
parūṣakaṃ varā drākṣā kaṭphalaṃ katakāt phalam 
rājāhvaṃ dāḍimaṃ śākaṃ tṛṇmūtrāmayavātajit   
añjanaṃ phalinī māṃsī padmotpalarasāñjanam 
sailāmadhukanāgāhvaṃ viṣāntardāhapittanut   
dv viṣāntardāhapittajit dv viṣāntardāhapittahṛt
paṭolakaṭurohiṇīcandanaṃ madhusravaguḍūcipāṭhānvitam 
nihanti kaphapittakuṣṭhajvarān viṣaṃ vamim arocakaṃ kāmalām   
guḍūcīpadmakāriṣṭadhānakāraktacandanam 
pittaśleṣmajvaracchardidāhatṛṣṇāghnam agnikṛt   
bv dhānyakāraktacandanam bv dhānyakaṃ raktacandanam
bv dhanikāraktacandanam
āragvadhendrayavapāṭalikākatiktānimbāmṛtāmadhurasāsruvavṛkṣapāṭhāḥ 
bhūnimbasairyakapaṭolakarañjayugmasaptacchadāgnisuṣavīphalabāṇaghoṇṭāḥ   
āragvadhādir jayati cchardikuṣṭhaviṣajvarān 
kaphaṃ kaṇḍūṃ pramehaṃ ca duṣṭavraṇaviśodhanaḥ   
dv medodaraviśodhanaḥ
asanatiniśabhūrjaśvetavāhaprakīryāḥ khadirakadarabhaṇḍīśiṃśipāmeṣaśṛṅgyaḥ 
trihimatalapalāśā joṅgakaḥ śākaśālau kramukadhavakaliṅgacchāgakarṇāśvakarṇāḥ   
asanādir vijayate śvitrakuṣṭhakaphakrimīn 
pāṇḍurogaṃ pramehaṃ ca medodoṣanibarhaṇaḥ   
bv śvitrakuṣṭhavamikrimīn
varuṇasairyakayugmaśatāvarīdahanamoraṭabilvaviṣāṇikāḥ 
dvibṛhatīdvikarañjajayādvayaṃ bahalapallavadarbharujākarāḥ   
av varaṇasairyakayugmaśatāvarī
varuṇādiḥ kaphaṃ medo mandāgnitvaṃ niyacchati

av varaṇādiḥ kaphaṃ medo cv adhovātaṃ śiraḥśūlaṃ

dv gulmamehakaphāpaham
vellantarāraṇikabūkavṛṣāśmabhedagokaṇṭaketkaṭasahācarabāṇakāśāḥ

bv gokaṇṭakotkaṭasahācarabāṇakāśāḥ cv

cv vṛkṣādanīnalakuśadvayaguñchagundrā cv

aśmarīśarkarāmūtrakṛcchrāghātarujāharaḥ

lodhraśābarakalodhrapalāśā jiṅginīsaralakaṭphalayuktāḥ

eṣa lodhrādiko nāma medaḥkaphaharo gaṇaḥ 
yonidoṣaharaḥ stambhī varṇyo viṣavināśanaḥ

surasayugaphaṇijjaṃ kālamālā viḍaṅgaṃ kharabusavṛṣakarṇīkaṭphalaṃ kāsamardaḥ

bv kharabukavṛṣakarṇīkaṭphalāḥ kāsamardaḥ bv
kharabusavṛṣakarṇīkaṭphalāḥ kāsamardaḥ bc
kharamukhavṛṣakarṇīkaṭphalaṃ kāsamardaḥ cv

kākamācī cv kṣavakasarasibhārgīkāmukāḥ kākamācī
cv kṣavakasvarasibhārgīkārmukāḥ kākamācī
surasādir gaṇaḥ śleṣmamedaḥkṛminiṣūdanaḥ 
pratiśyāyāruciśvāsakāsaghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ   
muṣkakasnugvarādvīpipalāśadhavaśiṃśipāḥ 
gulmamehāśmarīpāṇḍumedo'rśaḥkaphaśukrajit   
bv palāśadhavaśiṃśipam
vatsakamūrvābhārgīkaṭukā marīcaṃ ghuṇapriyā ca gaṇḍīram 
elā pāṭhājājī kaṭvaṅgaphalājamodasiddhārthavacāḥ

calakaphamedaḥpīnasagulmajvaraśūladurnāmnaḥ   
dv paśugandhā pañcakolakaṃ ghnanti
vacājaladadevāhvanāgarātiviṣābhayāḥ

bv āmātīsārapācanau
priyaṅgupuṣpāñjanayugmapadmāḥ padmād rajo yojanavally anantā

cv sāradrumo mocarasaḥ samaṅgā dv punnāmaśītaṃ
madanīyahetuḥ
ambaṣṭhā madhukaṃ namaskarī nandīvṛkṣapalāśakacchurāḥ

av nyagrodhapippalasadāphalalodhrayugma bv

Sūtrasthāna
guruśītasarasnigdhamandasūkṣmamṛdudravam 
auṣadhaṃ snehanaṃ prāyo viparītaṃ virūkṣaṇam   
sarpir majjā vasā tailaṃ sneheṣu pravaraṃ matam 
tatrāpi cottamaṃ sarpiḥ saṃskārasyānuvartanāt   
mādhuryād avidāhitvāj janmādy eva ca śīlanāt 
pittaghnās te yathāpūrvam itaraghnā yathottaram   
ghṛtāt tailaṃ guru vasā tailān majjā tato 'pi ca 
dvābhyāṃ tribhiś caturbhis tair yamakas trivṛto mahān   
svedyasaṃśodhyamadyastrīvyāyāmāsaktacintakāḥ 
vṛddhabālābalakṛśā rūkṣāḥ kṣīṇāsraretasaḥ

ūrustambhātisārāmagalarogagarodaraiḥ 
mūrchāchardyaruciśleṣmatṛṣṇāmadyaiś ca pīḍitāḥ

cv tatra dhīsmṛtimedhāgni
granthināḍīkṛmiśleṣmamedomārutarogiṣu

śeṣau vasā tu saṃdhyasthimarmakoṣṭharujāsu ca

niśy eva pitte pavane saṃsarge pittavaty api   
niśy anyathā vātakaphād rogāḥ syuḥ pittato divā 
yuktyāvacārayet snehaṃ bhakṣyādyannena vastibhiḥ   
nasyābhyañjanagaṇḍūṣamūrdhakarṇākṣitarpaṇaiḥ

yathoktahetvabhāvāc ca nācchapeyo vicāraṇā   
av snehasyānnābhibhūtatvād dv nācchaḥ peyo vicāraṇā

dvābhyāṃ caturbhir aṣṭābhir yāmair jīryanti yāḥ kramāt   
hrasvamadhyottamā mātrās tās tābhyaś ca hrasīyasīm 
kalpayed vīkṣya doṣādīn prāg eva tu hrasīyasīm   
hyastane jīrṇa evānne sneho 'cchaḥ śuddhaye bahuḥ 
śamanaḥ kṣudvato 'nanno madhyamātraś ca śasyate   
bṛṃhaṇo rasamadyādyaiḥ sabhakto 'lpo hitaḥ sa ca 
bālavṛddhapipāsārtasnehadviṇmadyaśīliṣu   
bv sabhakto 'lpo hitaś ca saḥ
strīsnehanityamandāgnisukhitakleśabhīruṣu 
mṛdukoṣṭhālpadoṣeṣu kāle coṣṇe kṛśeṣu ca   
prāṅmadhyottarabhakto 'sāv adhomadhyordhvadehajān 
vyādhīñ jayed balaṃ kuryād aṅgānāṃ ca yathākramam   
vāry uṣṇam acche 'nupibet snehe tat sukhapaktaye 
āsyopalepaśuddhyai ca taubarāruṣkare na tu   
mūrchā dāho 'ratis tṛṣṇā jṛmbhā mohabhramaklamāḥ

tenodgāraviśuddhiḥ syāt tataś ca laghutā ruciḥ

dravoṣṇam anabhiṣyandi nātisnigdham asaṃkaram

bv bhāṣyābhyāsanasaṃsthitīḥ bv bhāṣyātyaśanasaṃsthitīḥ
bv bhāṣyātyāśanasaṃsthitīḥ

bv rasabhuk svedam ācaran
ekāhaṃ dinam anyac ca kapham utkleśya tatkaraiḥ 
māṃsalā medurā bhūriśleṣmāṇo viṣamāgnayaḥ   
snehocitāś ca ye snehyās tān pūrvaṃ rūkṣayet tataḥ 
saṃsnehya śodhayed evaṃ snehavyāpan na jāyate   
alaṃ malān īrayituṃ snehaś cāsātmyatāṃ gataḥ 
bālavṛddhādiṣu snehaparihārāsahiṣṇuṣu   
yogān imān anudvegān sadyaḥsnehān prayojayet 
prājyamāṃsarasās teṣu peyā vā snehabharjitā   
dv peyā vā snehabharjitāḥ
tilacūrṇaś ca sasnehaphāṇitaḥ kṛśarā tathā 
kṣīrapeyā ghṛtāḍhyoṣṇā dadhno vā saguḍaḥ saraḥ   
av tilacūrṇaṃ ca sasneha bv phāṇitaṃ kṛśarā tathā
peyā ca pañcaprasṛtā snehais taṇḍulapañcamaiḥ 
saptaite snehanāḥ sadyaḥ snehāś ca lavaṇolbaṇāḥ   
dv snehaś ca lavaṇolbaṇaḥ

guḍānūpāmiṣakṣīratilamāṣasurādadhi

svedas tāpopanāhoṣmadravabhedāc caturvidhaḥ 
tāpo 'gnitaptavasanaphālahastatalādibhiḥ
